Nakayama Miki

He wahine Kepanī ʻo Nakayama Miki (hānau ʻo Maegawa Miki, 18 ‘Apelila 1798). Ua ho‘okumu ʻo ia o ka ho‘omana ‘o Tenrikyo.
Ua hānau ʻia ‘o ia ma Sanmaiden, Iāpana.





Georg Philipp Telemann

He haku mele ‘o Georg Philipp Telemann o nā mele Baroque.





William Shakespeare

He haku mele a he haku hana keaka Pelekane ‘o William Shakespeare (hānau 26 ‘Apelila 1564 – make 23 ‘Apelila 1616). ‘Ike ‘ia ‘oia e nā po‘e i ka mea kākau nui loa ma ka ‘ōlelo Pelekania. Kāna mau hana e ola ai e maupa‘a: 38 hana keaka, 154 sonnets, ame kekahi mau mele. Kapa ‘ia ‘o Shakespeare kō Pelekania haku mele ame ka "Bard of Avon." Ua unuhi ‘ia kāna mau hana keaka ma nā ‘ōlelo ola nui apau. 
Ua hānau ʻia ‘o Shakespeare ma Stratford-upon-Avon. Ke 18 ona makahiki, male ‘oia iā Anne Hathaway, aasdfasdfasdfasdfasdfasdfasdfasdfas ‘ekolu keiki kā lākou: Suzanna, Hamnet ame Judith. 
Mawaena o nā makahiki 1585 a 1592, ho‘omaka ‘oia he ‘oihana pono ma Lākana. Ma‘ō, he mea hana keaka a he mea kākau ‘oia. He ‘ona hapa ‘oia o ka ‘ahahui-hana keaka, ‘oia ho‘i, "Lord Chamberlain's Men" (loli ka inoa iā "King's Men"). Ua ho‘omaha loa ‘o Shakespeare iā Stratford ma ka makahiki 1613. Make ‘oia mahope aku o ‘ekolu makahiki. Kaka‘ikahi nā mo‘olelo o kō Spakespeare ola pilikino. Nui ka mana'o wale ‘ana o kāna mau hana a kāna mau mana‘o.
Hana ‘o Shakespeare i ka hapa nui o kāna mau hana i ‘ike ‘ia ai mawaena o nā makahiki 1590 a 1613. Nui nā mo‘olelo ame nā mo‘olelo le‘ale‘a o kāna mau hana keaka mua. Ā laila, nui nā mea kaumaha loa ā ka makahiki 1608. I kēlā manawa, kākau ‘oia iā Hamlet, King Lear ame Macbeth. 
Ua kākau ‘oia ‘ekolu ‘ano hana keaka: nā mo‘olelo, nā mo‘olelo le‘ale‘a, ame nā mea kaumaha loa.





Wolfgang Amadeus Mozart

He haku mele ko‘iko‘i ‘o Wolfgang Amadeus Mozart (27 Ianuali 1756 – 5 Kekemapa 1791; inoa piha Joannes Chrysostomus Wolfgangus Theophilus Mozart) o ka wā kelakikala. Makemake nui ‘ia ‘o Mozart o nā haku mele kelakikala.
Kona ola.
‘Ohana, wā li‘ili‘i.
Hānau ʻia ‘o Wolfgang Amadeus Mozart iā Leopold lāua ʻo Anna Maria Pertl Mozart i ke alanui Getreidegasse 9 ma Salzburg. ‘O Maria Anna (1751–1829) (kapakapa ‘ia "Nannerl") ke kaikuahine ho‘okahi wale nō o Wolfgang i ola ai mamua o ka hānau ʻia. Papekema ‘ia ‘o Wolfgang ma kēia lā a‘e ma St. Rupert's Cathedral. Kapa ka mo‘olelo papakema iā Mozart ‘o "Joannes Chrysostomus Wolfgangus Theophilus Mozart". Akā, ua kapa ‘o Mozart iā ia ‘o "Wolfgang Amadè Mozart". Nui nā ‘ano kona inoa.
He hope Kapellmeister kō Mozart makuakāne, Leopold Mozart, o ka hui ho‘okani pila aloali‘i o ka ‘akipihopa o Salzburg. He haku mele ‘o Leopold. He kumu ‘ike ‘ia ‘o ia; ma ka makahiki o ka hānau o Mozart, ua pa‘i ‘o ia i he puke a‘o holomua no ka pila, ‘o ia ho‘i, ‘o "Versuch einer gründlichen Violinschule".
I nā makahiki ‘ehiku o Nannerl, ha‘awi ‘o Leopold iā ia i nā ha‘awina no ka kulawie. Nānā ‘o Mozart i nā ha‘awina, me ka ho‘opunihei: ua mo‘olelo kona kaikuahine; ho‘ohala manawa ‘o ia i ka kulawie, loa‘a nā hapakolu, [...] a me hō‘ike kona le‘ale‘a i leo maika‘i ai [iā ia]."
Ua ho‘omau ‘o Nannerl: "i nā makahiki ‘ehā o Mozart, ua ho‘omaka kona makuakāne, like me he mea pā‘ani, e a‘o iā ia i he mau minuet a me he mau mele ma ke kulawie [...] hiki iā ia ke ho‘okani iā ia me kīnā ‘ole a me ka hune nui, a he pana hemolele kona. [...] nā makahiki ʻelima o Mozart, haku mele ‘ē ‘o ia i nā mele iki, i ho‘okani ai ‘o ia i kona makuakāne, i kākau iā lākou." ‘O kēlā mau mele ‘o Andante (K. 1a) a me ‘o Allegro in C (K. 1b).
‘Ī ka mea hō‘ike-ola Maynard Solomon, ‘oiai ‘o Leopold i he kumu aloha keiki, aia ka ‘ōlelo hō‘ike i hoʻoikaika ‘ia ai ‘o Wolfgang e holomua ma waho o nā ha‘awina o kona makuakāne. ‘O kō Mozart hana, kona mele mua, kū‘oko‘a (a me pakī me ka ‘īnika), a me kona hiki mua e ho‘okani i ka pila. Pū‘iwa ‘o Leopold. Pili ka makuakāne a me ke keiki kāne; hele mai kēia mau hanana iā Leopold ā hau‘oli.
Ke aniani ka no‘eau mele po‘okela o kana keiki kāne, hā‘awipio ‘o Leopold i ka haku mele.
‘O ia ke kumu wale nō o Wolfgang ma kona wā li‘ili‘i. A‘o ‘o Leopold i kana keiki i nā ‘ōlelo, nā kumuhana kula, a me ka mele ho‘okani.
1762-1773: Nā makahiki o ke ka‘ahele.
I ka wā o nā makahiki ho‘omohala o Mozart, hele kona ‘ohana i kekahi mau wahi ma ‘Eulopa. Ua hō‘ike ‘ia nā keiki. Ho‘omaka nā huaka‘i me he hō‘ikena ma ka makahiki 1762 ma ke Aloali‘i o ka ‘Elele Manakoho o Pawalia ma Munich, ā laila (ma ka makahiki like), ma ka Aloali‘i ‘Imepeliala ma Vienna a me Prague. Hele ka ‘ohana ma he ka‘apuni lō‘ihi (‘ekolu-hapalua makahiki) i nā aloali‘i o Munich, Mannheim, Palika, Lākana, The Hague, hele hou i Paris, a hele mai i ka home ma o Zürich, Donaueschingen, a me Munich. Ma kēia huaka‘i, hui ‘o Mozart i nā mea hoʻokani pila (he helu nui) a me kama‘āina iā ia me nā mele o kekahi mau haku mele. He ho‘ohuli mana‘o nui ‘o Johann Christian Bach iā Mozart. Hui lāua ma Lākana mai 1764–65. Hele hou ka ‘ohana i Vienna ma 1767 a ua noho ma‘ō ā Kēkēmapa 1768. 
Ho‘omāluhiluhi kēia mau huaka‘i, no ka mea o ke kūlana makakumu o ke ka‘ahele ma kēlā wā, ka pono e kali i nā palapala kono o nā ali‘i, a me nā ma‘i maika‘i ‘ole mamao o ka home. Ua ma‘i ka mākuakane ma Lākana ma ke kauwela o 1764, ā laila ua ma‘i nā keiki ‘elua ma The Hague ma ka hā‘ulelau o 1765.
Ma hope o ‘ekahi makahiki ma Salzburg, hele ‘o Leopold a me Wolfgang i Italy, a me noho mai i kō Wolgang makuahine a me ke kaikuahine ma ka home. Ho‘omaka ka huaka‘i ma Kēkēmapa 1769 a me ho‘opau ma Malaki 1771. Like me nā huaka‘i ma mua, ‘o ke kumu o kēia huaka‘i ka hō‘ike o nā hiki o Mozart me he mea ho‘okani a me he haku mele i ho‘omakua wiki ai. Hui ‘o Mozart iā Giovanni Batista Martini ma Bologna, a me ‘āpono ‘ia me he lālā o "Accademia Filarmonica". Ma Loma, ho‘olohe ho‘olua wale nō ‘o Mozart iā "Miserere" (na Gregorio Allegri) ma he hana ma Sistine Chapel, ā laila kākau piha ‘o ia iā ia mai ka hoʻomanaʻo ʻana, a ho‘i hou e ho‘opololei i nā hewa iki; pēlā, Hana ‘o Mozart i ke kope kolohe mua o kēia mele kia‘i ‘ia o ka Wakikana.
Ma Milana, ua kākau ‘o Mozart i ke keaka mele, ‘o "Mitridate Rè di Ponto" (1770), i kākela ‘ia ai. Ā laila, ho‘i mai nā uku komikina no ke keaka mele, a me ho‘i hou (‘elua manawa) ‘o Wolfgang a me ‘o Leopold mai Salzburg i Milan (‘Aukake-Kēkēmapa 1771, ‘Okakopa 1772-Malaki 1773) no ka haku mele a me nā ho‘omaka o "Ascanio in Alba" (1771) a me ‘o "Lucio Silla" (1772). Manaʻolana ‘o Leopold i hua ai kēia mau kipa ma he wae ‘oihana no kona keiki kāne ma ‘Ikalia, akā, ‘a‘ole hana ‘ia.
Ma ka ho‘opau o ka huaka‘i hope loa o ‘Ikalia, ua kākau ‘o Mozart i ka hana ho‘okani i hana ‘ia i kēia manawa, ka hīmeni kū pākahi cantata "Exsultate, jubilate", K. 165.
1773–1777: Ke aloali‘i o Salzburg.
Mahope o kona hele mai ‘ana hope loa me kona makuakāne mai ‘Ikalia (13 Malaki 1773), Hai ‘ia ‘o Mozart me he mea ho‘okani pila aloali‘i e ke ali‘i o Salzburg, ‘o Keiki Ali‘i-‘Akipihopa Hieronymus Colloredo. He kanaka punahele ‘o Mozart ma Salzburg. Ma ‘ō, nui kona hoaloha, a he manawa kūpono kona e haku ma nā ‘ano mahele (nā symphony, sonata, string quartet, serenade, a me keaka mele). I kō ‘oukou wā, hana ‘ia kekahi mau hana ho‘okani i hana ai ‘o ia i kēlā wā. Pēnei, i ka manawa ma waena o ‘Apelila a me Kēkēmapa o 1775, ho‘omōhala ‘o Mozart i he hoihoi no nā concerto no ka pila violina. Hana ‘o ia i nā concerto no ka pila violina ‘elima. Ma ka makahiki 1776, hana ‘o ia i nā concerto no ka piano.
I loko o kēia mau ho‘okō ‘ana, hele ‘o Mozart ā kaumaha i Salzburg a me hoʻoikaika e huli i he ‘oihana ma kahi ‘ē. ‘O ke kumu o ke kaumaha, kona uku hana iki, he mau 150 florin ma ka makahiki. Ho‘i, makemake ‘o Mozart e haku i nā keaka mele, a me kakaʻikahi ka hanana no ke keaka mele ma Salzburg. Ke ho‘opau ke keaka o ke aloali‘i ma 1775, ho‘omaika‘i ‘ole ke kūlana. Kahamaha nā huaka‘i ‘elua (no he ‘oihana) i ka noho ‘ana ma Salzburg. Kipa ‘o Wolfgang a me kona makuakāne iā Vienna (mai 14 Iulai - 26 Kepakemapa 1773), a me Munich (from 6 Kēkēmapa 1774 to Malaki 1775). ‘A‘ole holomua nā kipa, akā, i ka huaka‘i ma Munich, holomua ka ho‘omaka o kō Mozart keaka mele, "La finta giardiniera".
1777–1778: Ka huaka‘i ma Palika.
Ma ‘Aukake 1777, haʻalele ‘o Mozart i kona ‘oihana ma Salzburg a me hele aku (23 Kepakemapa) ma kekahi huaka‘i e huli i he ‘oihana, a me kipa iā Augsburg, Mannheim, Palika, and Munich. No ka mea o ka hō‘ole o ka ‘Akipihopa Colloredo e kala iā Leopold (e ka‘ahele me Mozart), kauoha ‘ia ka makuahine o Mozart, Anna Maria, e hele pū me ia. 
Ma Mannheim, kama‘āina ‘o Mozart me nā lālā o ka hui hoʻokani pila o Mannheim, ka hui hoʻokani pila nō ka ‘oi ma Europe i kēlā wā. Aloha ‘o ia iā Aloysia Weber, ke kahi o nā kaikamahine ‘ehā ma he ‘ohana mele. 
Aia he mau ‘oihana wehe ma Mannheim, akā, ‘a‘ole holomua ‘o ia, a hele ‘o Mozart i Palika (14 Malaki 1778) e huli hou. ‘A‘ole maika‘i kona pōmaikaʻi ma ‘ō; hō‘ike ke kahi o kona mau leka, aia he hā‘awi no he ‘oihana me he mea ‘okana ma Versailles, akā ‘a‘ole makemake ‘o Mozart i kēlā ‘oihana. Hele ‘o ia ā ‘ai‘ē a me pono e kū‘ai aku i nā waiwai. I ka manawa o ka huaka‘i, hele kō Mozart makuahine ā ma‘i a me make ‘o ia (3 Iulai 1778); Aia he mau ‘emo i loa‘a ke kauka; manaʻo wale ‘ia e Halliwell, aia ‘a‘ohe kālā.
I ka manawa i noho ‘o Wolfgang i Palika, huli ‘o Leopold i nā ‘oihana i ka home ma Salzburg no kona keiki kāne. Me ke kāko‘o o nā ali‘i kūloko, loaʻa he ‘oihana maika‘i e Leopold no Wolfgang, (me he mea ‘okana no ke aloali‘i a me haku o ka ‘aha hīmeni), me he uku hana o he mau 450 florin. 
Akā, kali ‘o Wolfgang e pani i kēia ‘oihana, a me ma hope o kona hele aku ‘ana mai Palika (26 Kepakemapa 1778), hele ‘o ia i Mannheim, ā laila ‘o Munich; manaʻolana ‘o ia i loa‘a he ‘oihana e ia ma waho o Salzburg. Ma Munich, hui hou ‘o ia iā Aloysia, he pu‘ukani holomua. ‘A‘ole aloha ‘o Aloysia iā Mozart.
Hele ‘o Mozart ma 15 Ianuali 1779 a me pani i kona ‘oihana hou. ‘A‘ole ‘olu‘olu ‘o ia ma Salzburg.
Ma ka huaka‘i ma Palika, kākau ‘o ia i kona mau mele kaulana; ‘o ia ho‘i, ka sonata no ka piano ma A minor, K. 310/300d, ma 1778; a me ka Symphony "Palika" (no. 31), ho‘okani ‘ia ma Palika ma nā lā 12 a me 18 Iune, 1778.
1781: Ka hele ‘ana ma Vienna.
Ma Ianuali 1781, holomua ka ho‘omaka o ke keaka mele,"Idomeneo", ma Munich. Keia Malaki a‘e, kēnā ‘ia ka haku mele iā Vienna, no ka mea, hele kona haku hana, ‘o Keiki ali‘i-‘Akipihopa Colloredo o Salzburg, i he hana hoʻohiwahiwa no ka ho‘okomo o Emperor Joseph II. Ke hana Colloredo iā Mozart me he kanaka hana, ame ke pāpā ‘ia ‘o Mozart e ka ʻakipihopa e ho‘okani no ka ‘Emepela ma ka aloali‘i o Countess Thun (‘o ka uku ka hapalua o kona uku o Salzburg), ho‘ohuhū ‘ia loa ‘o Mozart, he kanaka holomua ma Munich. Ma ka mahina o Mei, ho‘onui ua paio la: ho‘ā‘o ‘o Mozart e ha‘alele, akā hō‘ole ‘ia. Ma keia mahina a‘e, ‘Āpono ka ‘ae e hoʻi aku, akā hana ‘ia kūamuamu: Ho‘oku‘u ‘ia ‘o Mozart "me he peku ma ka ‘ōkole", i hana ‘ia e ke kuene o ka ‘Akipihopa, Kauna Arco. Ia wā nō, hō‘ike ‘o Mozart i nā manawa kūpono e ola maika‘i ma Vienna. Manaʻo ‘oia, pono ‘oia e noho ma‘ō ame ulu i kona ‘oihana. 
No Mozart, hana ‘ia pa‘akīkī ka paio me ka ʻAkipihopa e ka mea ‘oia‘i‘o i kōkua kona makuakāne i ka ‘ao‘ao o ka ʻAkipihopa: mana‘olana ‘oia i hele mai kana keiki kāne i ka manawa i ho‘i ‘o Colloredo. Kākau kona makuakane iā Wolfgang, ame ho‘olā‘au iāia e ʻuao me kō lāua haku hana. Makemake loa ‘o Wolfgang e hana ho‘okahi i kona ‘oihana ma Vienna. Ke hoʻokuʻu ‘ia ‘o Mozart, pau ka paio. Noa ‘o Mozart mai kona haku hana ame ke kauoha o kona makuakāne e ho‘i mai. Kapa ‘o Solomon i ke ka‘alele ‘ana o Mozart like me he "huliau nui", ame loli kō Mozart ola.
Ka wā mua ma Vienna.
Ho‘omaka maika‘i ka ‘oihana hou o Mozart. Ho‘okani pinepine ‘oia me he mea piano. ‘O kekahi hanana ka hoʻokūkū me Muzio Clementi no ka ‘Emepela ma 24 December 1781. Kākau ‘o New Grove, "‘o ia ka mea piano ‘oi loa ma Vienna." Ho‘i, hoʻowaiwai ‘o Mozart ame he haku mele: i ka wā o 1781–1782, kākau ‘oia i ke keaka mele ‘o "Die Entführung aus dem Serail" ("Ke Kā‘ili ‘Ana mai ka Seraglio"). Ho‘omaka ua keaka mele la ma 16 Iulai 1782 ame he holomua ‘oia. Ho‘okani ‘ia ke keaka mele "ma nā wahi i ‘ōlelo Kelemānia ma ‘Eulopa", ame ho‘okahua i ke kūlana o Mozart me he haku mele.
I ka manawa o kona paio me ‘Akipihopa Colloredo, ne‘e aku ‘o Mozart (1 Mei ai‘ole 2 Mei 1781) me ka ‘ohana Weber, i ne‘e ai mai Mannheim iā Vienna. Make ka makuakāne, ‘o Fridolin, ame kipa ka ‘ohana i nā mea māka‘ika‘i.
Male ‘o Aloysia, ka mea i aloha ‘ia e Mozart, me ka mea hana keaka ‘o Joseph Lange, pēlā, aloha ‘o Mozart i ke kaikamahine ‘ekolu, ‘o Constanze. Male lāua, me ka "‘ae kūʻē" o ka makuakane ‘o Leopold (New Grove), ma 4 ‘Aukake 1782. Hānau ‘o Constanze i nā keiki ‘eono; ola wale nō ‘elua keiki: ‘o Karl Thomas (1784–1858) ame ‘o Franz Xaver Wolfgang (1791–1844; he haku mele). 
I nā makahiki o 1782–1783, Ho‘okama‘āina ‘o Mozart i nā hana o J. S. Bach ame ‘o G.F. Handel no ka mea o ka hoʻololi o Baron Gottfried van Swieten, ka mea i kuleana i nā mele na nā mea ‘oi loa o ka wā Baroque.‘O ka hua o kō Mozart ho‘opa‘a o keia mau hana kekahi mau hana i hoʻopili i ke ‘ano Baroque, ame ho‘ololi loa i kana ‘ōlelo mele, like me nā paukū fugal ma "Die Zauberflöte" ("Ka ‘Ohe Kani Kalakupua"), ame ma ka hopena o Symphony 41. 
Ma 1783, kipa ‘o Wolfgang ame ‘o Constanze i ka ‘ohana o Mozart ma Salzburg, akā, ‘a‘ole holomau ke kipa. Ho‘omaka ke kipa i ka haku mele ‘ana o kekahi mele nui o Mozart, ‘o Mass in C Minor, i ho‘omaka ‘ia ma Salzburg (akā ‘a‘ole ho‘opau). Hīmeni ‘o Constanze ma ka ho‘omaka.
Mahope o kona ne‘e aku iā Vienna, hui ‘o Mozart iā Joseph Haydn ame ho‘āikāne lāua; nānā iā Haydn and Mozart. I ka manawa i kipa ‘o Haydn iā Vienna, ho‘okani pū lāua ma he string quartet ulu wale. Kākau ‘ia nā quartet ‘eono i ho‘ola‘a iā Haydn (K. 387, K. 421, K. 428, K. 458, K. 464, and K. 465) mai 1782–85, me he pane i kō Haydn Opus 33 mai 1781. I ka manawa i ho‘olohe ‘o Haydn i nā quartet o Mozart, ilihia ‘oia ame ‘ī iā Leopold, "Mamua o ke Akua ame me he kanaka pono, pono au e ha‘i iā ‘oe, ‘o kou keiki ka haku mele i ‘ike au: He kohu kona, ame, ka ‘ikena loa o ka haku mele ‘ana." I nā makahiki 1782–1785, ho‘okani ‘o Mozart i kona concert no ka piano me he leokū pāhaki ma kona mau ʻaha hīmeni.
Kākau ‘oia i nā concerto ‘ekolu ai‘ole ‘eha no kekahi kau ʻaha hīmeni, ame no ka mea o ke kaka‘ikahi o ka wehena ma nā hale keaka, hoʻokaʻawale ‘o Mozart i nā wahi ‘ē: he lumi nui ma Trattnerhof, he hale papa‘i; ame ka lumi hulahula o Mehlgrube, he hale ‘aina. Makemake nui ʻia nā ‘aha hīmeni
, ame kapa ‘ia nā concerto i haku mele ‘o Mozart i kona hana ‘oi loa. Kākau ‘o Solomon: i keia wā, hana ‘o Mozart i "he pili hui maika‘i ‘ana mawaena o he haku mele-mea ho‘okani ake ame he anaina māhie, i ha‘awi ‘ia ka manawa kūpono e nānā i ka ho‘ololi ame ka ho‘omaika‘i o ke ‘ano mele nui".
Me ke kālā nui i loa‘a e Mozart ma kona mau ‘aha hīmeni ame kekahi mau wahi, ola waiwai ‘oia ame ‘o Constanze. Ne‘e aku ka ‘ohana i he hale papa‘i pipi‘i, me he ho‘olimalima o he mau 460 florin. 
Kū‘ai mai ‘o Mozart i he fortepiano maika‘i mai Anton Walter no ke kumu kū‘ai o he mau 900 florin, a me he pākaukau pahupahu no ke kumu o he mau 300 florin. Kipaku ka ‘ohana Mozart i kekahi kaiki kāne ‘o Karl Thomas i ke kula pipi‘i ame mālama i nā kanaka hana. No ka mea o keia mau koho, ‘a‘ole waiwai ka ‘ohana Mozart ma nā makahiki mahope.
Ma 14 Kekemapa 1784, he Makona-Noa ‘o Mozart. Komo pae ‘oia i he hui malū ‘o "Zur Wohltätigkeit" ("Beneficence"). Nui Makona-Noa iā Mozart ma ka mahope o kona ola; hele i nā hālāwai, he Makona kekahi o kona aikāne, ame haku mele ‘o Mozart i nā mele Makona. E nānā iā: "Mozart ame Makona-Noa".
1786–1787: Ke keaka mele.
Holomua ‘o "Die Entführung aus dem Serail", akā, i nā makahiki mahope, kākau iki ‘o Mozart i nā keaka mele. Kākau ‘oia i nā keaka mele ‘elua i ho‘opau ‘ole ‘ia ai ame ka mahele-‘ekahi ‘o "Der Schauspieldirektor". I kēlā manawa, ‘o kona ‘oihana ka mea piano ame ka mea kākau i nā concerto. Akā, ma ka hope o 1785, huli ‘o Mozart i kona kakau ‘ana. Ho‘opau ‘oia e kākau ma‘amau i nā concerto no ka piano on a regular basis, ame ho‘omaka i kona hui ‘ana me ka mea mele Lorenzo da Ponte. Ma 1786, aia ka ho‘omaka ‘o "The Marriage of Figaro" ma Vienna. Holomua ke keaka mele ma Vienna, ame ma Prague ma ka hope o kēlā makahiki. Mahope o ka holomua ma Prague, aia he uku komikina no he keaka mele na Mozart ame Da Ponte, ‘o "Don Giovanni", i ho‘omaka ai ma 1787 me ka holomua ma Prague ame hana hou, ma Vienna ma 1788. ‘Ike ‘ia nā keaka mele ‘elua me nā hana mele nui o Mozart.
Ma Kekemapa 1787, loa‘a he ‘oihana aloali‘i e Mozart. Ho‘onoho ‘o ‘Emepela Iosepa II iāia me kona "haku mele chamber", he ‘oihana i ho‘ohāmama ‘ia ai ma ka mahina mamua a‘e i ka make o Gluck. Akā, he hapa-‘oihana. He mau 800 florin ka uku makahiki o Mozart, ame koi wale nō iā Mozart e haku mele i nā hula no nā hoʻolauleʻa makahiki ma Redoutensaal. Hoʻohalahala ‘o Mozart iā Constanze; ‘o ka uku, "nui no ko‘u hana, iki no he aha hiki ia‘u ke hana". Nui kēia uku, no ka mea, ke pa‘akikī kona ola, kōkua ke kālā. Hō‘ike nā mo‘olelo ‘aha: makemake ‘o Iosepa e hō‘oia‘i‘o, ‘a‘ole ‘o Mozart e hele aku mai Vienna e huli i nā ‘oihana maika‘i i kekahi wahi.
Ma 1787, hele ‘o Ludwig van Beethoven iā Vienna ame noho no ‘elua pule, no ka mea, makemake ‘oia e ho‘opa‘a me Mozart. i ka manawa o keia kipa, kū‘ē ka ‘ōlelo hō‘ike no he aha e hana. Aia ‘ekolu koho mua: Ho‘olohe ‘o Mozart i kō Beethoven ho‘okani ‘ana ame ho‘omaika‘i iāia, hō‘ole ‘o Mozart iā Beethoven me he haumana, ame ‘a‘ole hui lāua. (E nānā iā: "Mozart and Beethoven".)
1788–1790.
Ma ka hope o ke kekeke, mae ka ‘oihana o Mozart.
Ma 1786, ho‘opau ‘oia e ho‘okani pinepine ma nā ‘aha mele lehulehu, ame hā‘ule kona uku. No nā mea ho‘okani, pa‘akīkī keia wā ma Vienna no ka mea, aia ‘o Austria ma ke kaua, mae ka hoʻowaiwai ame ka hiki o nā ali‘i e kāko‘o i ka mele.
Ma ka waena o 1788, ne‘e aku ‘o Mozart ame kona ‘ohana mai Vienna i nā hale emi ma ka hu‘a o Alsergrund. Ho‘omaka ‘o Mozart e hō‘ai‘ē i ke kālā, pinepine mai kona hoaloha ame Makona Michael Puchberg; ola "he mahele o he mau leka mākilo" (New Grove). Hoʻopuka manaʻo ‘o Maynard Solomon; ‘eha ‘o Mozart i he kaumaha i kēlā manawa, ame ho‘oiki paha kona haku mele ‘ana. ‘O nā hana nui o keia wā, nā symphony ‘ekolu mahope loa (1788: 39, 40, 41; ‘a‘ole i ‘ike ‘ia inā ho‘okani kēia mau symphony ma ke ola o Mozart), ame ke keaka mele mahope loa o Mozart ame Da Ponte, "Cosi fan tutte", i ho‘omaka ‘ia ma 1790.
I keia wā, hele ‘o Mozart i nā huaka‘i lō‘ihi, no ka mea, makemake ‘oia e holomua i kona pōmaika‘i: he kipa ma ke kupulau o 1789 iā Leipzig, Dresden, ame Berlin (see: "Huaka‘i iā Berlin o Mozart"), ame he kipa ma 1790 iā Frankfurt, Mannheim, ame kekahi mau kūlanakauhale Kelemānia. Holomua iki keia mau kipa ame ‘a‘ole kōkua nā pilikia waiwai o Mozart.
1791.
Ma ka makahiki mahope loa o Mozart, ā kona ma‘i ame make, huahua nui ‘oia, ame (ma ka nānā o Maynard Solomon) ‘oia ka manawa o ke ola hou pilikino. I keia manawa, kākau ‘o Mozart i he mau mele nui, like kona hana i mahalo ‘ia: ke keaka mele "Ka ‘Ohe Kani Ho‘okalakupua", ka concerto no ka piano mahope loa (K. 595 in B flat), ‘o Concerto No Ke Kalioneke K. 622, ka mahope loa o kona string quintet (K. 614 ma E flat), ka motet Ave verum corpus K. 618, ame "Requiem" K. 626, i ho‘opau ‘ole ‘ia. 
Ho‘omaka e holomua ka waiwai o Mozart (‘o ia ke kumu o ka hopohopo ma 1790). ‘A‘ole maopopo loa ka ‘ōlelo hō‘ike, akā ho‘ohiki ka po‘e waiwai i mahalo iāia ma Hungary ame ma Amsterdam i nā uku makahiki iā Mozart, no ka haku mele. Ho‘owaiwai nui paha ‘o Mozart i ke kūa‘i aku o nā mele hula i kākau ai ‘oia no kona ‘oihana me he haku mele ‘imepeliala. Ho‘opau ‘oia e hō‘ai‘ē i ke kālā mai Puchberg ame ho‘omaka ‘oia e ho‘oka‘a.
Hō‘oluolu ‘o Mozart ma ka holomua o kona hana nui, ‘oia ho‘i, ‘o "Ka ‘Ohe Kani Ho‘okalakupua" (nui ka manawa o kona ho‘okani mawaena o ka wā o kona ho‘omaka ame kō Mozart make) ame "Little Masonic Cantata", K. 623, i ho‘omaka ai ma 15 Nowemapa, 1791.
Ka make.
"Nānā iā: Make o Mozart"
Hele ‘o Mozart ā ma‘i ma Prague. Aia ‘o Mozart ma‘ō no ka ho‘omaka ma 6 Kepakemapa o kona keaka mele ‘o "La clemenza di Tito", i kākau ‘ia ai ma 1791 ma ka uku komikina no ka poni mō‘i no ka ‘Emepela. Hiki ‘oia e ho‘omau i kona ‘oihana i wahi manawa; alaka‘i ‘oia i ka ho‘omaka o "The Magic Flute" ma 30 Kepakemapa. Ho‘olawehala ka ma‘i ma 20 Nowemapa, ame i kēlā manawa moe ma‘i ‘oia, ‘eha‘eha ‘oia i ka ‘ea kūka‘a ame ka lua‘i.
Mālama ‘ia ‘o Mozart ma kona ma‘i hope loa e Constanze, kona kaikaina muli loa ‘o Sophie, ame ke kauka o ka ‘ohana, ‘o Thomas Franz Closset. Aia ka ‘ōlelo hō‘ike, makemake nui loa kona mana‘o e ho‘opau i kona "Requiem". 
Li‘ili‘i ka pahiki, ha‘i ‘oia i ka mele iā Süssmayr.
Make ‘o Mozart ma ka hola ‘ekahi ma ke kahakiaka ma 5 Kekemapa. Penei ka hō‘ike ‘ano o New Grove e pili ana i kona ho‘olewa: "Kanu ‘ia ‘o Mozart i he hē ‘awelika, me ka mēheuheu hē Vienna i kēlā wā, ma ka ilina o St Marx mawaho o ke kūlanakauhale ma 7 Kekemapa. Inā (kākau nā hō‘ike hope) ‘a‘ole hele mai nā mea kanikau i kona hē, ‘oia me ka mēheuheu hē Vienna i kēlā wā; mahope, kākau ‘o Jahn (1856), aia ‘o Salieri, ‘o Süssmayr, ‘o van Swieten ame wiliwili kekahi mau mea ho‘okani ma ka hē. I kēlā lā, ‘a‘ole he ‘ino ame he hua; ‘olu‘olu ka lā."





Māhele:Haku mele (ho‘okani)

Eia nā haku mele i hana ai i nā mele ho‘okani.





Baharaina

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo Baharaina, kapa ʻia hoʻi Ke Aupuni Mōʻī o Baharaina aiʻole مملكة البحرين (i ka ʻōlelo ʻAlapia: "Mamlakat al-Baḥrayn"). Aia ʻo Baharaina ma ke Kai kūʻono Pelekia.

O‘ahu

‘O O‘ahu (kapakapa ‘ia "The Gathering Place") ka mokupuni nui ‘ekolu o nā mokupuni Hawai‘i. Nui loa ka po‘e i kēlā mokupuni ma ka moku‘āina Hawai‘i. Ma ke kapakai hikina hema ke kapikala o ka moku‘āina, ‘oia ho‘i, Honolulu. He 596.7 kapuaʻi kuea (1,545.4 klm²) ka nui o ua mokupuni la. A laila, ‘oia ka mokupuni nui loa iwakālua ma ka ‘Amelika Hui. He lō‘ihi o 44 mile a he ākea o 30 mile kō keia mokupuni pele. He 227 mile ka lō‘ihi o ke kahakai. Ua hana ‘ia ‘o O‘ahu e nā lua pele kuahene ‘elua, ‘oia ho‘i, ‘o Wai‘anae a ‘o Ko‘olau. ‘O ka wahi luna loa o ka mokupuni ka mauna Ka‘ala (4,003 kapua‘i maluna o ke kai). Aia ka mauna ma ka pae-kuahiwi Wai‘anae.





Luakini ma Lā‘ie, Hawai‘i

‘O ka Luakini ma Lā‘ie, Hawai‘i (ma ka ‘ōlelo Pelekane: "Laie Hawaii Temple"), mamua "Hawaiian Temple" ai‘ole "Hawaii Temple" (Luakini Hawai‘i), ka luakini o ka ʻEkalekia Molemona. Aia ka luakini ma ke kahakai hikina ‘ākau o ka mokupuni o O‘ahu, ma ke kūlanakauhale o Lāʻie (he 35 mile mai Honolulu). Me ke Alanui Brigham Young ma Hawaii a ke Polynesian Cultural Center, nui ka luakini ma ke kūlanakauhale.
‘O ka Luakini ma Lā‘ie ka luakini mua loa o ka ʻEkalekia Molemona i hana ‘ia ai mawaho o ka ‘Amelika mokuhonua, ka luakini kahiko loa mawaho o ka moku‘āina o Utah, ame ka luakini lima-mua loa o ka ʻEkalekia Molemona i hana ai. Ho‘ola‘a ‘ia ka wahi o ka luakini e ka pelekikena-ʻekalekia Joseph F. Smith ma 1 Iune 1915, ame ho‘ola‘a ‘ia ka hale ma 27 Nowemapa 1919 e ka pelekikena-ʻekalekia Heber J. Grant. Mamua, ‘o ka "Hawaiian Temple" ai‘ole ka "Hawaii Temple" ka inoa o ka luakini ā nā makahiki 2000.
Mōʻaukala.
Lāʻie.
Ua kūʻai mai ka ʻEkalekia i he mahi kō me 6,000 ʻeka (24 klm) ma 1865.





Josepa Samika

Josepa Samika





Luakini ma Kona, Hawai‘i

‘O ka Luakini ma Kona, Hawai‘i (ma ka ‘ōlelo Pelekane: "Kona Hawaii Temple") ka luakini kanahiku o ka ʻEkalekia Molemona. ‘O ia ka luakini ‘elua ma Hawai‘i, mahope o ka Luakini ma Lā‘ie, Hawai‘i. Aia ua luakini la i Kailua-Kona, ma ka mokupuni o Hawai‘i. Ho‘ola‘a ‘ia ka wahi o ka luakini e John B. Dickson ma 13 Malaki 1999, ame ho‘ola‘a ‘ia ka hale ma 23 Ianuali 2000 e ka pelekikena-ʻekalekia Gordon B. Hinckley.





Māhele:‘Ōlelo

Eia nā ‘ōlelo o ke ao nei.





Kaua‘i

‘O Kaua‘i (‘ōlelo ‘ia [kauˈaʔi] ma ka ‘ōlelo Hawai‘i ma‘amau; [tauˈaʔi] ma ka ‘ano ‘ōlelo Kauaʻi-Niʻihau; /ˈkaʊɑɪ/ or /kaʊˈɑɪ/ a pela ‘ia "Kauai" mawaho o nā mokupuni Hawai‘i) ka mokupuni kahiko loa o nā mokupuni Hawai‘i. He 552.3 kapuaʻi kuea (1,430.5 km²) ka nui o Kaua‘i. ‘Oia ka mokupuni ‘ehā-nui loa o nā mokupuni ‘ano nui ma ka pae‘āina Hawai‘i, a ka mokupuni ‘iwakāluakūmākahi-nui loa ma ka ‘Amelika Hui. Kapakapa ‘ia iā "Garden Isle". Aia he 105 mile (170 kilomekele) o ke kōwā Kaua‘i mawaena o Kaua‘i a ‘o O‘ahu. ‘O Kawaikini ka wahi luna loa o ka mokupuni mauna (he 5,243 kapuaʻi ka luna). ‘O ka mauna Wai‘ale‘ale ka wahi ‘elua-luna loa, (he 5,148 kapuaʻi ka luna). ‘O ua mauna la kekahi wahi pulu loa ma ka Honua, me ka ua ‘awelika makahiki o he 460 ‘īniha (11,700 mm). ‘A‘ole ‘ike ‘ia ka mana‘o kapakapa o Kaua‘i.





Pokémon

‘O Pokémon ka franchise pāpaho. No ka hui pā‘ani wikiō Nintendo ‘o Pokémon. Ua hana ‘ia ‘oia e Satoshi Tajiri.





Ni‘ihau

‘O Ni‘ihau (kapakapa ʻia ʻo "The Forbidden Isle" i ka ʻōlelo Pelekane; "Ka Moku Kapu" i ka ʻōlelo Hawaiʻi) ka mokupuni iki loa o nā mokupuni o Hawai‘i i noho ‘ia ai i ka moku‘āina o Hawai‘i ma ‘Amelika Hui. 69.5 kapua‘i kuea a ko Niʻihau ‘alea. Aia ‘o Ni‘ihau ma ke komohana hema o Kaua‘i, ā hiki i he mau mile 17.5. Aia ke alawai Kaulakahi mawaena o Kaua‘i a ‘o Ni‘ihau. Aia ka mokupuni ʻo Lehua ma ka ‘ao‘ao ‘ākau o Ni‘ihau (ā hiki i he mau mile 0.7). Aia kekahi loko kūlohelohe o Hawai‘i ma Ni‘ihau, ‘oia ho‘i, ka loko ʻo Halulu. No Keith Robinson lāua ʻo Bruce Robinson ʻo Ni‘ihau.





Māhele:Mokupuni o Hawai‘i

Eia nā mokupuni o Hawai‘i.





Hawai‘i (mokupuni)

‘O ka mokupuni o Hawai‘i (kekahi inoa i ka ‘ōlelo Pelekane: Big Island, Hawai‘i Island) ka mokupuni pele i ko ‘Amelika Hui moku‘āina o Hawai‘i ma ka moana Pākīpika. 4,028 kapua‘i kuea (10,432 klm²) a ko Hawaiʻi ‘alea o ua mokupuni la. ‘Oia ka mokupuni nui loa ma ‘Amelika Hui. Nui ka ‘alea ‘o Hawai‘i mamua o ka ‘alea o nā mokupuni o Hawai‘i āpau. ‘Ōlelo ‘ia i kapa ‘ia ai ka mokupuni e ka inoa Hawaiʻiloa, ka hoʻokele Polenekia i hō‘ike ‘ia ai i nā mokupuni o Hawai‘i. Hoʻoponopono ‘ia ka mokupuni o Hawai‘i e ke kalana o Hawai‘i. ‘O Hilo ka noho kalana. Koho ‘ia ma ka makahiki 2003, aia he mau kanaka 158,400 ma Hawai‘i.





Maui

‘O Maui ka mokupuni nui lua o nā mokupuni o Hawai‘i. 727.2 kapua‘i kuea (1883.5 klm²) o ko Maui ‘alea. ‘Oia ka mokupuni nui loa ‘umikūmāhiku ma ‘Amelika Hui. Aia ‘o Maui ma loko o ka moku‘āina o Hawai‘i, a ka mokupuni nui loa ma ke kalana o Hawai‘i. Aia kekahi mokupuni ‘ekolu, ‘oia ho‘i, Lāna‘i, Kaho‘olawe, a me Moloka‘i, ma ke kalana. ‘O "Maui Nui" ka inoa o nā mokupuni pū ‘ehā. Ma ka makahiki 2000, 117,644 a Maui poʻe. ‘O Kahului ke kūlanakauhale nui loa ma ka mokupuni. ‘O Wailuku ka noho kalana.





Kaho‘olawe

‘O Kaho‘olawe ka mokupuni iki loa o nā mokupuni ‘ewalu o Hawai‘i. He lō‘ihi o 11 mile a he ākea o 6 mile kō keia mokupuni. He 44.6 mile kuea (115.5 km²) ka ‘alea o ka mokupuni. ‘O ka wahi luna loa ka lua o Lua Makika ma ka luna o Puʻu Moaulanui (1,477 kapua‘i maluna o ke kai) Aia ua mokupuni la ‘ehiku mile mai ka ‘ao‘ao komohana hema o Maui.





Wikipedia:Nā lula kepela

To ensure consistency in spelling ("kepela"), please follow the following guidelines regarding spelling of Hawaiian words. These guidelines were proposed by ʻAhahui ʻŌlelo Hawaiʻi in 1978.





Lāna‘i

‘O Lāna‘i (‘ōlelo ‘ia [lɑːnɑʔi]) ka mokupuni nui loa ‘eono o nā mokupuni o Hawai‘i. Kapakapa ‘ia ka "Pineapple Island", no ka mea, i ka wā mamua, he mahi hala kahiki ‘o Lāna‘i. Aia kekahi kūlanakauhale iki, ‘oia ho‘i, ‘o Lana‘i City. He 18 mile ke ākea o ka mokupuni. He 140.5 kapua‘i kuea (364 km²) ka ‘alea. A laila, ‘oia ka mokupuni nui loa kanahākūmālua ma ‘Amelika Hui. Aia ke alawai Kalohi mawaena o ua mokupuni la ame ‘o Moloka‘i. Aia ke alawai ‘Au‘au mawaena o Lāna‘i ame ‘o Maui. Ma ka makahiki 2000, aia 3,193 po‘e ma Lāna‘i.





Pelelina

‘O Pelelina (ai‘ole Berelina) ke kapikala o Kelemānia. He kūlanakauhale nui loa ia.





Moloka‘i

‘O Moloka‘i (‘ōlelo Pelekane: "Molokai") ka mokupuni nui loa ‘elima o nā mokupuni o Hawai‘i. ‘Oia ka mokupuni nui loa iwakāluakūmāhiku ma ‘Amelika Hui. He 38 ame 10 mile ka lō‘ihi ame ke ākea. He 260 mile kuea ka ‘alea. Aia ke alawai Ka‘iwi (he 25 mile ka lō‘ihi) mawaena o Moloka‘i a ‘o O‘ahu (ma ka ‘ao‘ao komohana). Aia ke alawai Kalohi mawaena o Moloka‘i a ‘o Lāna‘i (ma ka ‘ao‘ao hema).





Lākana

‘O Lākana ke kapikala o ke Aupuni Mōʻī Hui Pū ʻia.





Kakalameko

‘O Kakalameko ke kapikala o Kaleponi.





Wailele ‘o Niakala

He wailele ka wailele ‘o Niakala. Aia ka wailele ma ke kahawai ‘o Niakala.





Wakinekona

He moku‘āina ‘o Wakinekona o ‘Amelika Hui Pū ‘ia. ‘O ‘Olumepia ke kapikala o Wakinekona.





‘Olekona

He moku‘āina ‘o ‘Olekona o ‘Amelika Hui Pū ‘ia. ‘O Kalema ke kapikala o ‘Olekona.





Kololako

He moku‘āina ‘o Kololako o ‘Amelika Hui Pū ‘ia.





Nū Mekiko

He moku‘āina ‘o Nū Mekiko o ‘Amelika Hui Pū ‘ia. ʻO Santa Fe ke kapikala o Nū Mekiko. ʻO ʻAlepukaka ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o Nū Mekiko.





Kekeka

He moku‘āina ‘o Kekeka o ‘Amelika Hui Pū ‘ia. ʻO Austin ke kapikala o Kekeka. ʻO Houston ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o Kekeka.





Pololika

He moku‘āina ‘o Pololika o ‘Amelika Hui Pū ‘ia.





‘Okalahoma

He moku‘āina ‘o ‘Okalahoma o ‘Amelika Hui Pū ‘ia. ‘O Kūlanakauhale o ‘Okalahoma ke kapikala o ‘Okalahoma.





Nepalaka

He moku‘āina ‘o Nepalaka o ‘Amelika Hui Pū ‘ia.





Kanekaka

He moku‘āina ‘o Kanekaka o ‘Amelika Hui Pū ‘ia. ‘O Kopika ke kapikala o Kanekaka.





Uka

He moku‘āina ‘o Uka o ‘Amelika Hui Pū ‘ia.





‘Ikahō

He moku‘āina ‘o ‘Ikahō o ‘Amelika Hui Pū ‘ia.





Monekana

He moku‘āina ‘o Monekana o ‘Amelika Hui Pū ‘ia.





Waiomina

He moku‘āina ‘o Waiomina o ‘Amelika Hui Pū ‘ia. ʻO Kene ke kapikala o Waiomina.





‘Akanaka

He moku‘āina ‘o ‘Akanaka (ʻōlelo Pelekane: "Arkansas") o ‘Amelika Hui Pū ‘ia. Aia ʻo ia ma ka hema o ʻAmelika Hui. ‘O Little Rock ke kapikala a me ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o ‘Akanaka. ʻO ka ʻōlelo Pelekane ka ʻōlelo kūhelu o ʻAkanaka.





Kakoka ‘Ākau

He moku‘āina ‘o Kakoka ‘Ākau o ‘Amelika Hui Pū ‘ia. ʻO Bismarck ke kapikala o Kakoka ʻĀkau. ʻO Fargo ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o Kakoka ʻĀkau.





Kakoka Hema

He moku‘āina ‘o Kakoka Hema o ‘Amelika Hui Pū ‘ia.





Minekoka

He moku‘āina ‘o Minekoka o ‘Amelika Hui Pū ‘ia. ʻO Paulo Kaneka ke kapikala o Minekoka. ʻO Mineapoli ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o Minekoka.





‘Iowa

He moku‘āina ‘o ‘Iowa o ‘Amelika Hui Pū ‘ia. ‘O Kemoine ke kapikala o ‘Iowa.





Mikouli

He moku‘āina ‘o Mikouli o ‘Amelika Hui Pū ‘ia.





Luikiana

He moku‘āina ‘o Luikiana o ‘Amelika Hui Pū ‘ia. ‘O Pakona Luka ke kapikala o Luikiana.





Mikikipi

He moku‘āina ‘o Mikikipi o ‘Amelika Hui Pū ‘ia.





‘Alapama

He moku‘āina ‘o ‘Alapama (i ka ʻōlelo Pelekane: "Alabama") o ‘Amelika Hui Pū ‘ia. ʻO Montgomery ke kapikala o ʻAlapama. ʻO Birmingham ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o ʻAlapama.





Keokia (‘Amelika Hui Pū ‘ia)

He moku‘āina ‘o Mikikana o ‘Amelika Hui Pū ‘ia.

Wilikinia

Melelana

He moku‘āina ‘o Melelana o ‘Amelika Hui Pū ‘ia.





Maine

He moku‘āina ‘o Maine o ‘Amelika Hui Pū ‘ia.





Welemoneka

Nū Hamekia

He moku‘āina ‘o Nū Hamekia o ‘Amelika Hui Pū ‘ia. ʻO Concord ke kapikala o Nū Hamekia. ʻO Manakekeka ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o Nū Hamekia.

Nuioka

He moku‘āina ‘o Nuioka (‘Ōlelo Pelekania: New York) o ‘Amelika Hui Pū ‘ia. ‘O ‘Alapani ke kapikala o Nuioka.





Nū ‘Ieleke

He moku‘āina ‘o Nū ‘Ieleke o ‘Amelika Hui Pū ‘ia.





Penekelewinia

He moku‘āina ‘o Penekelewinia o ‘Amelika Hui Pū ‘ia.





Kelawea

He moku‘āina ‘o Kelawea o ‘Amelika Hui Pū ‘ia.





Wilikinia Komohana

He moku‘āina ‘o Wilikinia Komohana o ‘Amelika Hui Pū ‘ia.





Halakepoka

He kūlanakauhale ‘o Halakepoka. ‘O ia ke kapikala o Konekikuka.





Końskowola

He kūlanakauhale ‘o Końskowola ( : [kɔɲskɔ'vɔla]) ma hikina hema o Pōlani. Ho‘onoho ‘ia mawaena o Puławy ame Kurów, ma ke kahawai Kurówka. He kapikala ia o he aupuni kiwikā ("gmina") hemo, maloko o ka panalā‘au ("Voivodeship") Lublin. Aia 2,188 po‘e (o 2004) ma ke kūlanakauhale.





Makulu

‘O Makulu ka hōkū hele ‘eono mai ka lā ma ke kahua o nā hōkū. He mau komo lau kā Makulu.





Mineapoli

ʻO Mineapoli (ʻŌlelo Pelekane: "Minneapolis") ke kūlanakauhale nui loa i ka kaumokuʻāina o Minekoka. Aia ʻo Mineapoli ma luna o nā kapa o ke Kahawai Mikikipi. Pili ʻo Mineapoli me Kaneka Paulo, ke kapikala o Minekoka.





ʻĀtoma

He huna iki loa ka ʻātoma o ke kumumea kemikala.





Kumulipo

He oli ke Kumulipo e pili ana i ke kumu honua o ka honua.





Kamehameha

ʻO Kamehameha ka inoa o:
Hiki iā Kamehameha ke pili i:





Hōʻole Akua

Hō‘ole Akua, Mahuakala 
Aia kekahi mau kānaka. mana‘o‘i‘o ‘ole i ke Akua o nā Hoʻomana Kalikiano, Iukaio, a me Mohameka, a i ‘ole, i nā akua ‘ē a‘e like ‘ole a pau. Hilinaʻi naʻe lākou i ke kālaiakuhi a Kale Darwin ʻo ia hoʻi ke Liliuewe ʻana.

Pokekona

ʻO Pokekona ke kapikala a me ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o Makakukeka.





Aupuni kiwikā

He holoʻokoʻa luna hoʻohana ʻo ke aupuni kiwikā.





‘Ane‘ālika

ʻO ‘Aneʻālika ka ʻāinapuniʻole hema loa o Honua.





Iāpana

He ʻāina ʻo Iāpana (日本 aiʻole 日本国) ma ka hikina o ʻĀkia. ʻO Tokyo ke kapikala o ia ʻāina. Aia ʻo ia i ka Moana Pākīpika ma ka hikina o ke Kai ʻo Iāpana, Kina, Kōlea ʻĀkau, Kōlea Hema, a me Lūkia. He pae moku ʻo Iāpana me 3,000 mau moku. ʻO nā moku nui loa ʻehā ʻo Honshū, ʻo Hokkaidō, ʻo Kyūshū, a me Shikoku. ʻŌpalipali a pele kekahi mau moku. ʻO ka pūʻuo o Iāpana ka pūʻuo nui loa ʻumi i ka honua.





‘Aukekulelia

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo ʻAukekulelia a i ʻole Nūhōlani. ʻO ʻAukekulelia ka ʻāinapuniʻole iki loa o ka honua. Aia ʻo ʻAukekulelia ma ka poepoe hapa hema. ʻO Canberra ke kapikala o ʻAukekulelia. ʻO Kikinē ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o ʻAukekulelia.





Palakila

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo Palakila, kapa ʻia hoʻi "Brasil" aiʻole "República Federativa do Brasil" i ka ʻōlelo Pokukala. Aia ʻo Palakila ma ʻAmelika Hema. ʻO Brasília ke kapikala o Palakila. ʻO São Paulo ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o Palakila.





Māhele:Panalā‘au o Salamanca






Pōmare I

‘O Pōmare I ka mō‘ī mua o Kahiki ma waena o nā makahiki 1788? a me 1791. ‘O Tu-nui-ea-i-te-atua-i-Tarahoi Vairaatoa Taina Pomare I kona inoa ma ka pela kahiko a i ‘ole ‘o Tū-nui-ʻēʻa-i-te-atua ma ka pela hou. Ua hānau ‘ia ‘o ia ma Pare. ‘O Teu Tunuieaiteatua kona mākua kāne a ‘o Tetupaia-i-Hauiri kona makuahine.





Pōmare II

‘O Pōmare II (1782-7 Kekemapa 1821) ka mō‘ī ‘elua o Kahiki. ‘O Tu Tunuieaiteatua Pomare II kona inoa ma ka pela kahiko a i ‘ole ‘o Tū Tū-nui-ʻēʻa-i-te-atua Pōmare II ma ka pela hou.





Pōmare III

‘O Pōmare III (1820-1827) a i ‘ole ‘o Teriʻi-ta-ria Pōmare III ka mō‘ī ‘ekolu o Kahiki ma waena o nā makahiki 1821 a me 1827. ‘O ke keiki kāne ‘elua a Pōmare II ‘o ia. Ua hānau ‘ia ‘o ia i Papa‘oa ma ‘Ārue ma ka lā 25 o Iune 1820 a ua papekema ‘ia ma ka lā 10 o Kepakemapa 1820. Ua poni mō‘ī ‘ia ‘o Pōmare III i Papa‘oa ma ‘Ārue ma ka lā 21 o ‘Apelila 1824. Ua hele ‘o ia i ke kula ‘o South Sea Academy i Papetoai ma Mo‘orea.





‘Ārue

‘O ‘Ārue kekahi kaona ukali o Pape‘ete ma Kahiki. E noho ana 9,458 kānaka ma ‘Ārue ma ka makahiki 2007.





Pōmare IV

‘O Pōmare IV (28 Pepeluali 1813 - 17 Kepakemapa 1877) a i ‘ole ‘o ʻAimata Pōmare IV Vahine-o-Punuateraʻitua ka mō‘ī wahine o Kahiki ma waena o nā makahiki 1827 a me 1877. ‘O ke kaikamahine a Pōmare II ‘o ia.





Mo‘ai

He ki‘i kanaka pōhakukūkahi ka mo‘ai ma ka mokupuni Polenekia o Rapa Nui. Ua kālai ‘ia kēia mau ki‘i ma waena o nā makahiki 1250 a me 1500. He mau kānaka nui kekahi a he mau po‘o kānaka nunui wale nō kekahi. Kaulana ‘o Rapa Nui i nā mo‘ai. Ke koe nei ka hapalua o nā mo‘ai ma ka lua ‘eli pōhaku nui ‘o Rano Raraku a ua hali ‘ia kekahi hapalua i nā "ahu" o ka mokupuni. ‘O ka hua‘ōlelo Rapa Nui ke "ahu" no ke kahua o ka mo‘ai.
‘A‘ole i mōakāka ke kumu no ka hina ‘ana o nā mo‘ai a me ka ho‘opau koke ‘ana o ke kālai pōhaku ‘ana.





Hōkūleʻa

He waʻa kaulua ʻo Hōkūleʻa. Na Polynesian Voyaging Society i kūkulu iā ia i ka makahiki 1975. ʻO ka lā 8 Malaki 1975 ka lā o ko Hōkūleʻa holo ʻana hoʻokahi.





Hanauma

He kūʻono ʻo Hanauma ma Oʻahu. Aia ʻo Hanauma ma ke kapakai hikina hema o Oʻahu.





Hanauma (mele)

He mele Hawaiʻi ʻo Hanauma e pili ana no ke kūʻono o Hanauma. ʻO Mary Kawena Pukui ka haku mele o "Hanauma". ʻO Maddy Lam ke kūkulu puolo o ia.
Nā lila.
Mahalo aʻe ana au
I ka nani aʻo Hanauma
Ke kai kūʻono hālaʻi
Pōʻai ʻia e nā pali
Ua makemake nui ʻia
Ke alanui kīkeʻekeʻe
E iho aku ai i lalo
I ke kaha one ākea
He kahua na ka lehulehu
E luana hauʻoli ai
E hoʻolono like aʻe ana
I ka leo hone o ke kai
ʻOluʻolu i ka peʻahi
A ka makani aheahe
E hoʻoluli mālie nei
I na lau aʻo ke kiawe
Haʻina mai ka puana
No ka nani aʻo Hanauma
Ke kai kūʻono hālaʻi
Pōʻai ia e nā pali





Pauoa

He kaiahome ʻo Pauoa, a i ʻole ka Awāwa Pauoa, ma Honolulu, Hawaiʻi.
He mau kula kā Pauoa:





‘Ālaka

He mokuʻāina ʻo ʻĀlaka o ʻAmelika Hui Pū ʻia. ʻO Juneau ke kapikala o ʻĀlaka.





Kāneʻohe

He kūlanakauhale ʻo Kāneʻohe ma Oʻahu, Hawaiʻi. 34,970 poʻe a Kāneʻohe ma ka helu kanaka 2000.





Haleakalā

He lua pele kuahene ʻo Haleakalā ma Maui, Hawaiʻi.





Wikipedia:ʻOkina

The ʻokina is a Hawaiian letter. The ʻokina style that should be used on Wikipikia is still debated, but it is generally agreed that either ‘ or ʻ should be used, and "not" an apostrophe (') or a tick (`). To type ʻokina, you can do the following:
It is possible for an automated bot to convert all instances of apostrophes, ticks, and the template to an ʻokina.





Pae moku

He pae a i ʻole he ʻāhui ka pae moku o nā moku.
Pae moku ʻo Hawaiʻi, Iāpana, a me Aupuni Mōʻī Hui Pū ʻia.





Moana Pākīpika

ʻO ka Moana Pākīpika ka moana nui loa o Honua.





Kahiki

He moku ʻo Kahiki ma Polenekia Palani.





ʻOlumepika Kauwela ma 2008

He hanana haʻuki kauʻāina nā pāʻani ʻOlumepika Kauwela ma 2008. Aia ʻo ia ma Beijing, Kina mai 8 ʻAukake i 24 ʻAukake 2008.





Beijing

ʻO Beijing (i ka ʻōlelo Pākē: 北京) ke kapikala o Kina. Aia ka ʻOlumepika Kauwela ma 2008 ma Beijing.





Puʻuhonua o Hōnaunau

He puʻuhonua ʻo Puʻuhonua o Hōnaunau ma Hawaiʻi.





Kīlauea

ʻO Kīlauea ka lua pele ʻā wale nō o Hawaiʻi. Aia ʻo Kīlauea ma kō ka mokupuni o Hawaiʻi hikina hema.





Waipahu

He kūlanakauhale ʻo Waipahu ma ka moku o ʻEwa ma Oʻahu, Hawaiʻi.





Kartlis Deda

He kiʻi ʻo Kartlis Deda (i ka ʻōlelo Keokia: ქართლის დედა) ma Tbilisi, Keokia.





Māhele:Mauna o Hawaiʻi

Eia nā mauna o Hawaiʻi.





Huki ʻIa

He mele Hawaiʻi ʻo Huki ʻIa na Kakaʻe Kaleiheana. Hīmeni kēia mele e ʻAi Pohaku. ʻO kēia mele e pili ana no ka hae Hawaiʻi a me ka hae ʻAmelika Hui. He lila ʻo "huki ʻia lā i luna" o kēia mele. Haʻi kēia mele e huki o ka hae Hawaiʻi ma luna o ka hae ʻAmelika Hui.

Ma hea hou aʻe kū pono a e hoʻi<br>

Hōkū hele

He mea ʻano lani ka hōkū hele. E ka wehewehe ʻana, pōʻai nā hōkū hele e puni i ka hōkū.





Makelika

ʻO Makelika ke kapikala a me ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o Sepania.





‘Ōlelo Kahiki

‘O ka ‘ōlelo Kahiki ("te reo tahiti" a i ‘ole "te reo mā‘ohi") kekahi ‘ōlelo kūhelu o Polenekia Palani me ka ‘ōlelo Palani. ‘O ka ‘ōlelo Kahiki kekahi ‘ōlelo Polenekia Hikina a he ‘ōlelo ‘ano like me ka ‘ōlelo Rarotonga, ka ‘ōlelo Māori o Aotearoa a me ka ‘ōlelo Hawai‘i.





Kapikala

He ʻalea aupuni ke kapikala.





‘Apekanikana

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo ʻApekanikana (i ka ʻōlelo Pelekia: جمهوری اسلامی افغانستان) ma ʻĀkia waena. ʻO Kabul ke kapikala a me ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o ʻApekanikana.





Kina

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo Kina (i ka ʻōlelo Kina: 中國 a i ʻole 中国), a i ʻole ka ʻĀina Pākē, ma ka hikina o ʻĀkia. ʻO Beijing ke kapikala o Kina. ʻO Kanahai ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o Kina.





Hiliuma

‘O hiliuma ke kumumea kemikala ‘elua.





Likiuma

‘O likiuma ke kumumea kemikala ‘ekolu.





Beryllium

‘O beryllium ke kumumea kemikala ‘ehā.





Boron

‘O boron ke kumumea kemikala ‘elima.





Kalepona

‘O kalepona ke kumumea kemikala ‘eono.





Naikokene

‘O naikokene ke kumumea kemikala ‘ehiku.





‘Okikene

‘O ‘okikene ke kumumea kemikala ‘ewalu.





Fluorine

‘O fluorine ke kumumea kemikala ‘eiwa.





Eaʻula

‘O eaʻula (nīane) ke kumumea kemikala ‘umi.





Sodiuma

‘O sodiuma ke kumumea kemikala ‘umikūmākahi.





Makanekiuma

‘O makanekiuma ke kumumea kemikala ‘umikūmālua.





‘Aluminuma

‘O ‘aluminuma ke kumumea kemikala ‘umikūmākolu.





Silikone

‘O silikone ke kumumea kemikala ‘umikūmāhā.





Pokepola

‘O pokepola ke kumumea kemikala ‘umikūmālima.

‘O sulufura ke kumumea kemikala ‘umikūmāono.

‘O kolorine ke kumumea kemikala ‘umikūmāhiku.

‘O ‘aragona ke kumumea kemikala ‘umikūmāwalu.

Titanium

‘O titanium ke kumumea kemikala iwakāluakūmālua.





Kumumea kemikala

He ʻātoma ke kumumea kemikala.





Waikīkī

He ʻāpana ʻo Waikīkī o Honolulu, Hawaiʻi. ʻO ka Ala Wai ka palena ʻākau a me ka palena komohana o Waikīkī. ʻO Lēʻahi ka palena hikina.





Kaimukī

He ʻāpana ʻo Kaimukī o Honolulu, Oʻahu.





Moana ʻAkelanika

ʻO ka Moana ʻAkelanika ka moana nui lua o ka honua.





Moana ʻIniana

He moana ka Moana ʻIniana.





Moana ʻĀlika

ʻO ka Moana ʻĀlika ka moana iki loa o ka honua.





Māhele:Nā moana

Eia nā moana o ka Honua.





Alanui ʻo Kamehameha

‘O ke Alanui ʻo Kamehameha kekahi alanui nui ma O‘ahu.





‘Ōlelo Palani

I kēia manawa, ‘ōlelo ‘ia ka ‘ōlelo Palani (i ka ʻōlelo Palani: "français", ) e nā mānaleo 65-80 miliona, ame e ka po‘e 190-200 miliona me he ‘ōlelo ‘elua al‘ole ‘ekolu. Nui ka po‘e i ‘ōlelo Palani ma nā ‘āina kanalimakūmāhā. Noho nā mānaleo hapa loa o ka ‘ōlelo iā Palani, ke kumu o ka ‘ōlelo. Noho kekahi mau kanaka iā Kanaka, Pelekuima, Kuikilana, Lukemapuka, Monako, ai‘ole ma ‘Amelika Hui.





‘Akepaikana

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo ʻAkepaikana (i ka ʻōlelo ʻAkepaikana: "Azərbaycan") ma ʻEulopa a me ʻĀkia. ʻO Baku ke kapikala o ʻAkepaikana.





ʻAnakola

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo ʻAnakola ma ʻEulopa. ʻO Andorra la Vella ke kapikala o ʻAnakola.





ʻAukekulia

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo ʻAukekulia, a i ʻole ʻAuseturia, ma ʻEulopa. ʻO Vienna ke kapikala o ʻAukekulia.





‘Amelika

ʻO ʻAmelika ka inoa o:





Louvre

‘O ka Hale Hō‘ike‘ike o Louvre (‘ōlelo Palani: Musée du Louvre) ka hale hō‘ike‘ike hana no‘eau i kipa ‘ia nui loa, he pāka kiaho‘omana‘o aupuni, ame he hō‘ailona aupuni. Aia ka hale hō‘ike‘ike ma Palika, Palani. Aia ka hale hō‘ike‘ike mawaena o ke kahawai Seine ame Rue de Rivoli i ka Ho‘āhua ‘Ākau ma ke kaiahome o ke arrondissement kahi.





Mokupuni

He ʻāina hoʻokaʻawale ʻia ka mokupuni.





Sonata No. 8 no Piano (Beethoven)

Na Ludwig van Beethoven i haku mele iā Sonata No. 8 no Piano ma C māina, op. 13, kapa ‘ia me Pathétique. Pa‘i ‘ia ma 1799, akā, kākau ‘ia ma 1798, i he mau iwakāluakūmāwalu makahiki o ia. Ua ho‘ola‘a ‘o Beethoven i ka sonata i kona hoaloha, Prince Karl von Lichnowsky.





Māmā

Ma ka mana‘o mele, ‘o māmā ka manawa o kekahi hana mele. Nui loa ma he hana mele, no ka mea, hiki ke ho‘ololi i ka na‘au ame ka pa‘akikī o kekahi hana mele. ‘O ka helu nui o "māmā" ma ka ‘ōlelo Ikalia ‘o "tempi", akā, ma ka ‘ōlelo Pelekania, ‘ōlelo ‘ia ho‘i ‘o "tempos".





‘Ao‘ao Kū‘oko‘a Pokoliko

‘O ka ‘Ao‘ao Kū‘oko‘a Pokoliko (‘ōlelo Kepania: "Partido Independentista Puertorriqueño", PIP) kekahi ‘ao‘ao Pokoliko i paipai kalaiʻāina no ke kū‘oko‘a o Pokoliko mai ‘Amelika Hui. ‘O ia kekahi o nā ‘ao‘ao ‘ekolu nui ma Pokoliko ame ka ‘ao‘ao kahiko ‘elua ma‘ō.





Wiekanama

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo Wiekanama (i ka ʻōlelo Wiekanama: "Việt Nam") ma ka hikina hema o ʻĀkia. ʻO Hanoi ke kapikala o Wiekanama.





Hiʻiaka

He akua wahine Hawaiʻi ʻo Hiʻiaka (a i ʻole Hiʻiakaikapoliopele). ʻO Haumea lāua ʻo Kāne kona mau mākua. ʻO ia ke akua o hula. Ua hāpai ʻo ia ma Kahiki i ka hua, akā, ua hānau ʻia ʻo Hiʻiaka ma Hawaiʻi. ʻO ia ke kaikaina punahele o Pele.





Pele

He akua wahine Hawaiʻi ʻo Pele. ʻO Haumea lāua ʻo Kāne kona mau mākua. ʻO ia ke akua o ke ahi, ka uila, a me nā lua pele. Lawe ka inoa o nā lua pele mai ko Pele inoa. Noho ʻo ia ma Halemaʻumaʻu, Kīlauea.





Oboe

‘O ke Oboe kekahi pila ho‘okani o nā woodwind. ‘Elua ‘ohe a ke oboe. Mamua o ka makahiki 1770, kapa ‘ia (ma ka ‘ōlelo Pelekania), ‘oia ho‘i, "hautbois", "hoboy", ai‘ole "French hoboy". Hele mai ke kepela o "oboe" ma ka ‘ōlelo Pelekania ~1770 mai ke kepela Ikalia, "oboè", he unuhina o ka ho‘opuka o ke kepela Palani, "hautbois". ‘O "hautbois" ka huaʻōlelo hoʻohui ʻia o "haut" ("luna, leo nui") ame "bois" ("lā‘au, woodwind"). ‘O kekahi mea ho‘okani pila i ho‘okani i ke oboe ka mea oboe.





‘Ohe kani

‘O ka ‘ohe kani kekahi pila ho‘okani o nā woodwind. ‘Ohe ‘ole a ka ‘ohe kani. Aia ke kani mai ke kahe o ke ea ma he ka‘e. ‘O kekahi mea ho‘okani pila i ho‘okani i ka ‘ohe kani ka mea ‘ohe kani.





‘Alekina

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo ʻAlekina (ʻōlelo Sepania: "República Argentina") ma ʻAmelika Hema. ʻO Buenos Aires ke kapikala o ʻAlekina.





Kaumokuʻāina

He mahele kālaiʻāina ke kaumokuʻāina.





Banagaladesa

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo Banagaladesa ma ʻĀkia. ʻO Dhaka ke kapikala o Banagaladesa.





Pelekiuma

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo Pelekiuma ma ʻEulopa. ʻO Palukela ke kapikala o Pelekiuma.





‘Aikupika

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo ʻAikupika (‘Ōlelo ‘Alapia: مصر) ma ʻApelika. ʻO Kailo ke kapikala o ʻAikupika.





‘Aikiopia

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo ʻAikiopia ma ʻApelika. ʻO Addis Ababa ke kapikala o ʻAikiopia.





Palani

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo Palani ma ʻEulopa. ʻO Palika ke kapikala o Palani.





‘Īnia

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo ʻInia ma ʻĀkia. ʻO Delhi Hou ke kapikala o ʻInia.





‘Inidonesia

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo ʻInidonesia (ʻōlelo ʻInidonesia: "Republik Indonesia") ma ʻĀkia. ʻO Jakarta ke kapikala o ʻInidonesia.





‘Ilana

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo ʻIlana (ʻōlelo Pelekia: ايران) ma ʻĀkia. ʻO Tehran ke kapikala o ʻIlana.





‘Ilaka

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo ʻIlaka (ʻōlelo ʻAlapia: جمهورية العراق) ma ʻĀkia. ʻO Baghdad ke kapikala o ʻIlaka.





ʻAkenai

ʻO ʻAkenai (ʻōlelo Helene: Αθήνα) ke kapikala o Helene.





Lehua

He moku iki ʻo Lehua i 0.7 mau mile ma ka ʻākau o Niʻihau. He puʻu hakuhune ʻo ia. 284 a Lehua ʻakele.





Wikipedia:Papela

He mau anakuhi ʻo Papela no nā ʻōlelo mea hoʻohana.





Mokupuni o Hawai‘i

He pae moku nā mokupuni o Hawaiʻi, kapa ʻia nā mokupuni Kanauika i ka wā ma mua, ma waena o ka Moana Pākīpika. 19 mokupuni a me mokupuni pālahalaha ko ka pae moku. ʻO Hawaiʻi ka mokupuni hema loa, a ʻo Mokupāpapa ka mokupuni pālahalaha ʻākau loa.





Wikipikia

He puke noiʻi kūʻikena ʻo Wikipikia.





Lahaina

He ʻāpana ʻo Lahaina ma Maui, Hawaiʻi. ʻO ia ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o Maui. 11,704 poʻe a Lahaina ma ka helu kanaka 2010. Aia ʻo ia ma ka hema o Kāʻanapali, Nāpili-Honokōwai, a me Kapalua. ʻO Lahaina ke kapikala kahiko o ka Aupuni Mōʻī o Hawaiʻi.





Kakaʻako

He ʻāpana ʻo Kakaʻako o Honolulu, Hawaiʻi.





Nā mokuʻāina o ʻAmelika Hui

ʻO ka mokuʻāina o ʻAmelika Hui ka mokuʻāina o ka ʻāina o ʻAmelika Hui Pū ʻia. Kanalima mokuʻāina o ʻAmelika Hui Pū ʻia.





Māhele:Nā mokuʻāina o ʻAmelika Hui

Eia nā mokuʻāina o ʻAmelika Hui.





Kilo hōkū

He akeakamai ke kilo hōkū. Kilo kēia akeakamai i nā hōkū, nā hōkūhele, nā hōkū puhipaka, a me nā wiliau hōkū.





Kālailau nahele

He akeakamai ke kālailau nahele. Kilo kēia akeakamai i nā meakanu, nā ola o nā meakanu, a me ka hoʻomōhala ʻana o nā meakanu.





Kālaikaiaola

He akeakamai ke kālaikaiaola i ka ola.

He akeakamai ke kālaikūlohea i nā meakino a me ka ʻoni o nā meakino.

San Vicente del Raspeig

Nā kiaʻāina o Hawaiʻi

He papa inoa kēia o nā kiaʻāina o Hawaiʻi a me ka Panalāʻau o Hawaiʻi. ʻO ke kiaʻāina ka ilāmuku o ka mokuʻāina a me ka ʻalihikaua nui o ko mokuʻāina pūʻali koa.
Koho ʻia ke kiaʻāina i ka noho ʻana no ʻehā makahiki. Hoʻomaka ka noho ʻana ma ka Pōʻakahi mua loa o Kēkēmapa.
ʻO Linda Lingle ke kiaʻāina ʻeono o ka mokuʻāina o Hawaiʻi. Ua koho ʻia ʻo ia ma 2002 a ua koho ʻia hou ʻo ia ma 2006. ʻO ia ke kiaʻāina wahine mua loa a me ke kiaʻāina Iukaio mua loa.
Nā kiaʻāina.
Ua pākuʻi ka Lepupalika o Hawaiʻi na ʻAmelika Hui Pū ʻia ma 1898. Ua kūkulu ʻo ia i ka Panalāʻau o Hawaiʻi ma 1900. Ua hoʻokomo ʻo ia i ʻAmelika Hui ma 1959. ʻO Sanford B. Dole ka pelekikena wale nō o ka Lepupalika.
Nā kiaʻāina o ka Lepupalika.
Ua kūkulu ka Lepupalika o Hawaiʻi ma 14 Iune 1900.





Kōkua:Papa kuhikuhi

Kālaiʻōlelo

Bemmel e ho‘ololi nei iā Kālaiʻōlelo Nederland i ho‘ololi ‘ia ‘oe ‘a‘ole 12.192 ololi nei iā





Hawaiʻi Ponoʻī

ʻO Hawaiʻi Ponoʻī ka mele hīmeni o ka mokuʻāina o Hawaiʻi. Na Kalākaua i kākau i nā huaʻōlelo o kēia mele i ka makahiki 1874. Ua haku ʻia kēia mele e Kāpena Henri Berger. Hīmeni pinepine ʻia kēia mele ma nā hoʻokūkū haʻuki, ma hope o ka mele aupuni o ʻAmelika Hui. 
Nā lila.
Hawaiʻi ponoʻī

Kamehameha I

ʻO Kamehameha I ke aliʻi mua o ke Aupuni Mōʻī o Hawaiʻi. Ua naʻi ʻo ia i nā mokupuni a pau o Hawaiʻi a nāna i hoʻokumu i ke Aupuni Mōʻī o Hawaiʻi pae ʻāina. ʻIke ʻia ʻo Kamehameha i kē kānāwai o Māmalahoe. ʻO "Kalani Paiʻea Wohi o Kaleikini Kealiʻikui Kamehameha o ʻIolani i Kaiwikapu kaui Ka Liholiho Kūnuiākea" ko Kamehameha inoa piha.





Māmalahoe

He kānāwai ʻo Māmalahoe o ka Aupuni Mōʻī o Hawaiʻi. Ua hoʻokumu ʻia ʻo Kamehameha I i kēia kānāwai ma 1797 ma Puna. ʻĀpono kēia kānāwai i loko o ke kumukānāwai Hawaiʻi ma ka mea ʻeiwa, ma ka paukū ʻumi.
Aia ke kikokikona o ke kānāwai ma lalo:





Hoʻolele hualono

O ka hoolele hualono ka hoāhu o nā waihona leo ma ka pūnaewele. Ua hoohuaōlelo ia kēia huaōlelo e Keola Donaghy.





Hae

He ʻīāole ka hae.





Aupuni

ʻO ke "'aupuni," he 'aha ia e mālama ana i ka ʻaoʻao kālaiʻāina o kekahi lāhui paha, mokuʻāina paha a pēlā aku. ʻO ia ka mea nānā e ʻāpono i nā kānāwai e hahai ʻia e ka lehulehu.





ʻAlea

He kuaniki ka ʻalea o he ʻili kinona papa.





Likepona

ʻO Likepona (ʻōlelo Pokukala: "Lisboa") ke kapikala a me ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o Pokukala.





Mokekao

ʻO Mokekao (ʻōlelo Lūkia: Москва́) ke kapikala a me ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o Lūkia. ʻO ia ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o ʻEulopa.





Hunakalia

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo Hunakalia (ʻōlelo Hunakalia: "Magyar Köztársaság") ma ʻEulopa. ʻO Budapest ke kapikala a me ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o Hunakalia.





ʻIlelani

He ʻāina ʻo ‘Ilelani (‘ōlelo ‘Ilelani: "`Éire") ma ʻEulopa. ʻO Kupelina ke kapikala a me ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o ‘Ilelani.





Kenemaka

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo Kenemaka (ʻōlelo Kenemaka: "Kongeriget Danmark") ma ʻEulopa. ʻO Kopenahakena ke kapikala a me ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o Kenemaka.





Kuekene

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo Kuekene (ʻōlelo Kuekene: "Konungariket Sverige") ma ʻEulopa. ʻO Kekokehome ke kapikala a me ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o Kuekene.





Kuikilani

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo Kuikilani (ʻōlelo Kelemānia: "Schweiz", ʻōlelo Palani: "Suisse", ʻōlelo ʻĪkālia: "Svizzera", ʻōlelo Romānia: "Svizra") ma ʻEulopa. ʻO Berne ke kapikala o Kuikilani. ʻO Zürich ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o Kuikilani.





Kupelo

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo Kupelo (ʻōlelo Helene: Κύπρος, ʻōlelo Kuleke: "Kıbrıs") ma ʻEulopa. ʻO Nicosia ke kapikala a me ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o Kupelo.





Likenekaina

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo Likenekaina (ʻōlelo Kelemānia: "Fürstentum Liechtenstein") ma ʻEulopa. ʻO Vaduz ke kapikala o Likenekaina. ʻO Schaan ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o Likenekaina.





Lukemapuka

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo Lukemapuka (ʻōlelo Lukemapuka: "Groussherzogtum Lëtzebuerg", ʻōlelo Palani: "Grand-Duché de Luxembourg", "Großherzogtum Luxemburg") ma ʻEulopa. ʻO Lukemapuka ke kapikala a me ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o Lukemapuka.





Pulukalia

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo Pulukalia (ʻōlelo Pulukalia: България) ma ʻEulopa. ʻO Sofia ke kapikala a me ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o Pulukalia.





ʻĀina Pilipino

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo ka ʻĀina Pilipino ma ʻĀkia. ʻO Manila ke kapikala o ka ʻĀina Pilipino. ʻO ke Kūlanakauhale o Kekona (Quezon) ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o ʻĀina Pilipino.





Panamā

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo Panamā (ʻōlelo Sepania: "República de Panamá") ma ʻAmelika Waena. ʻO ke Kūlanakauhale o Panamā ke kapikala a me ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o Panamā.





ʻĀina Hau

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo ʻĀina Hau (ʻōlelo ʻĀina Hau: "Ísland" a i ʻole "Lýðveldið Ísland") ma ʻEulopa. ʻO Reykjavík ke kapikala a me ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o ʻĀina Hau. 321,857 a ʻĀina Hau poʻe ma ka helu kanaka o 2013.





ʻUkelena

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo ʻUkelana (ʻōlelo ʻUkelana: Україна) ma ʻEulopa. ʻO Kiev ke kapikala a me ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o ʻUkelana.





ʻIseraʻela

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo ʻIseraʻela ma ʻĀkia. ʻO Ielukalema ke kapikala a me ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o ʻIseraʻela.





Kaikikana

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo Kaikikana (ʻōlelo Kaikikana: Кыргызстан) ma ʻĀkia. ʻO Bishkek ke kapikala a me ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o Kaikikana.





Kamabodia

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo Kamabodia ma ʻĀkia. ʻO Phnom Penh ke kapikala a me ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o Kamabodia.





Kasakana

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo Kasakana (ʻōlelo Kasakana: Қазақстан) ma ʻĀkia. ʻO Astana ke kapikala o Kasakana. ʻO Almaty ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o Kasakana.





Katala

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo Katala (ʻōlelo ʻAlapia: قطر) ma ʻĀkia. ʻO Doha ke kapikala a me ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o Katala.





Johann Sebastian Bach

‘O Johann Sebastian Bach (hoʻopuka ‘ia: joˈhan/ˈjoːhan zeˈbastjan ˈbax) (21 Malaki 1685 – 28 Iulai 1750) ka haku mele Kelemania ame ka mea ʻokana i kākau i nā hana no‘eau no ka papa hīmeni, no ka hui hoʻokani pila, ame no nā mea pa‘ahana. No ka mea o kona hana, hele ka mele o ka wā Baroque ā makua piha.





Villalbos

He aupuni kiwikā ‘o Villalbos, i ka panalā‘au o Burgos, ma Castille a Leon, ma Sepania.
Villalbos
Video o Villalbos 1 (2008) 
Video o Villalbos 2 (2008)





Ludwig van Beethoven

‘O Ludwig van Beethoven ("‘ōlelo Pelekania:" ˈlʊdvɪg væn ˈbeɪtoʊvən; "‘ōlelo Kelemānia:" ˈluːtvɪç fan ˈbeːthoːfn, 16 Kekemapa 1770 – 26 Malaki 1827) ka haku mele Kelemānia ame ka mea piano. He ka‘apeha ‘oia ma ka wā mawaena o ka wā Classical ame ka wā Romantic ma ka mele classical.





Barack Obama

Ola mua.
Ua hānau ʻia ʻo Barack Obama i ka lā 4 ʻAukake, 1961 ma Kapiʻolani Medical Center ma Honolulu, Hawaiʻi. ʻO Barack Obama Makua lāua ʻo Ann Dunham nā inoa o kona mau mākua. No Nyang’oma Kogelo, Kenia mai kona makuakāne a no Wichita, Kanekaka mai kona makuahine.
Ma hope o kō Ann Dunham ʻoki male ʻana mai Barack Obama Makua, ua male ʻo ia iā Lolo Soetero a ua hele aku ʻo Barack keiki lāua ʻo Ann i ko Soetero one hānau ʻo ʻInidonesia ma ka makahiki 1967. Ua hele ʻo Barack i kekahi mau kula kūloko ma laila e like me St. Francis of Assisi School ma Jakarta. Ua hoʻi mai ʻo Barack i Hawaiʻi a ua noho ʻo ia me kona mau kūpuna, ʻo Madelyn lāua ʻo Stanley Dunham. Ua hele ʻo Barack i ke kula ʻo Punahou mai ka papa ʻelima a hiki i kona puka kula ma ka makahiki 1979.





Poʻe Hawaiʻi

ʻO ka poʻe Hawaiʻi, kapa ʻia nā kānaka ʻōiwi, nā kānaka maoli, a i ʻole nā Hawaiʻi maoli, nā poʻe Polenekia o ka papa kūʻauhau Hawaiʻi.





Ua Mau ke Ea o ka ʻĀina i ka Pono

ʻO Ua Mau ke Ea o ka ʻĀina i ka Pono ka mākia o ka mokupuni o Hawaiʻi.





Mauna Loa

ʻO Mauna Loa ka luapele nui loa ma ka honua. He luapele kuahene ʻā ʻo ia o ka mokupuni o Hawaiʻi. Iki loa ka silaka mai nā luaʻi pele.





Mauna Kea

He luapele ʻo Mauna Kea o ka mokupuni o Hawaiʻi. ʻO ia ka mauna lōʻihi loa ma ka honua, akā, ʻaʻole ʻo ia ka mauna kiʻekiʻe loa. He luapele kuahene kaʻoko ʻo ia.





Hualālai

He luapele kuahene kaʻoko ʻo Hualālai o ka mokupuni o Hawaiʻi. ʻO ka wēkiu o Hualālai ma 8,271 kp ma luna o ka ʻilikai.





Waiʻaleʻale

He mauna ʻo Waiʻaleʻale ma Kauaʻi, Hawaiʻi. ʻO ka wēkiu o Waiʻaleʻale ka wahi ua nui loa o ka honua, me ka ʻawelika o 460 mau ʻīn i nā makahiki 32 i hala o kēia makahiki.





Papaʻāpoho

He moku iki ʻo Papaʻāpoho ma Papahānaumokuākea ma nā mokupuni Hawaiʻi komohana ʻākau. 384.425 ʻeka ā Papaʻāpoho.





Mary Kawena Pukui

He kanaka Hawaiʻi ʻo Mary Abigail Kawenaʻulaokalaniahiʻiakaikapoliopelekawahineʻaihonua Wiggin Pukui (1895-1986). Ua ike ʻia ʻo ia ʻo Kawena. He meaʻimi naʻauao, haku mele, a me mea hula ʻo ia. Ua hānau ʻia ʻo ia ma Kaʻū, Hawaiʻi. ʻO Mary Paʻahana Kanakaʻole (he Hawaiʻi) lāua ʻo Henry Wiggin (he kanaka mai Makakukeka) nā inoa o kona mau mākua.
He mea hula kona kupuna wahine i ke aloaliʻi o Mōʻī Wahine Emma. He kahuna lāʻau lapaʻau a he kahuna pale keiki kona kupuna kāne. Ua lomilomi, lāʻau lapaʻau, hoʻoponopono, a pule ʻo ia. He kahuna pule ke kupuna wahine kualua i ke kūʻauhau o Pele.
Ua hele ʻo Pukui i ke Kula Mikiona Hawaiʻi. Ua aʻo ʻo ia ma ke Kula o Punahou. He mānaleo ʻo Pukui i ka ʻōlelo Hawaiʻi. Ua unuhi ʻo ia i nā ʻōlelo noʻeau mai kona makahiki 15. Ua hana ʻo ia ma ka Hale Hōʻikeʻike o Kamehameha mai 1938 i 1961. He mea kōkua ʻo ia i ka noiʻi ponoʻana o ke kūlana o ke kanaka a me nā unuhi. Ua paʻi ʻo ia i nā palapala 50, like me "Hawaiian-English Dictionary" (ka puke wehewehe Hawaiʻi), "Place Names of Hawaiʻi" (nā inoa wahi o Hawaiʻi), a me "ʻŌlelo Noʻeau". He puke noiʻi ʻo "Nānā i ke Kumu, Look to the Source", kona puke paʻi ʻia, o nā mēheuheu Hawaiʻi.





Kaʻū

ʻO Kaʻū ka ʻāpana hema loa o ka mokupuni o Hawaiʻi.





Thulium

ʻO thulium ke kumumea kemikala kanaonokūmāiwa.





Māhele:Kumumea kemikala

Eia nā kumumea kemikala.





Kuete

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo Kuete (ʻōlelo ʻAlapia: دولة الكويت‎) ma ʻĀkia. ʻO ke Kūlanakauhale o Kuete ke kapikala a me ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o Kuete.





Laosa

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo Laosa ma ʻĀkia. ʻO Wīanakana (ʻōlelo Pakalao: "ວຽງຈັນ" wīangchan, ʻōlelo Pelekane: "Vientiane") ke kapikala a me ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o Laosa.





Lepanona

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo Lepanona (ʻōlelo ʻAlapia: لبنان) ma ʻĀkia. ʻO Beirut ke kapikala a me ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o Lepanona.





Maladiwa

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo Maladiwa ma ʻĀkia. ʻO Malé ke kapikala a me ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o Maladiwa.





Malaisia

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo Malaisia ma ʻĀkia. ʻO Kuala Lumpur ke kapikala a me ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o Malaisia.





Monokolia

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo Monokolia (ʻōlelo Monokolia: Монгол улс, ) ma ʻĀkia. ʻO Ulan Bator ke kapikala a me ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o Monokolia.





Nepala

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo Nepala (ʻōlelo Nepali: नेपाल) ma ʻĀkia. ʻO Kathmandu ke kapikala a me ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o Nepala.
President: Bidhya Devi Bhandari (2015)
Prime Minister: Khadga Prasad Sharma Oli (2015)





Pakitana

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo Pakitana (ʻōlelo Urdu: پاکستان) ma ʻĀkia. ʻO Islamabad ke kapikala o Pakitana. ʻO Karachi ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o Pakitana.





Puruma

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo Puruma ma ʻĀkia. ʻO Nepido ke kapikala o Puruma. ʻO Ianagona (Ranagūna) ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o Puruma.





Sililanaka

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo Sililanaka ma ʻĀkia. ʻO Sri Jayawardenapura-Kotte ke kapikala o Sililanaka. ʻO Colombo ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o Sililanaka.





Sinapoa

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo Sinapoa (ʻōlelo Pākē: 新加坡, ʻōlelo Malaia: "Singapura") ma ʻĀkia.





Tailani

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo Tailani (ʻōlelo Tailani: ราชอาณาจักรไทย) ma ʻĀkia. ʻO Panekoka ke kapikala a me ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o Tailani.





Kenia

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo Kenia ma ʻApelika. ʻO Nairobi ke kapikala a me ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o Kenia.





Kula ʻo Punahou

He kula ʻo Punahou, kapa ʻia ke Kulanui ʻo Oʻahu i ka wā ma mua, ma Honolulu, Hawaiʻi.





Kula ʻo Kamehameha

He kula ʻo Kamehameha ma Hawaiʻi. ʻEkolu kahua o Kamehameha: ma Kapālama, ma Pukalani, a ma Keaʻau. Hoʻokahua ʻo Kamehameha na kā Bernice Pauahi Bishop palapala kauoha.
Papa Kūmole.
 





Bernice Pauahi Bishop

He aliʻiwahine Hawaiʻi ʻo Bernice Pauahi Bishop (hānau ʻia ma Kēkēmapa 19, 1831 – make ma ʻOkakopa 16, 1884). Ua hoʻokahua ʻo ia i ke kula ʻo Kamehameha me kāna palapala kauoha.
'O Abner Paki kona makuakane. A 'o Laura Konia kona makuahine. 'O ia, ke mo'opuna o Kamehameha I.





Halemaʻumaʻu

He lua pele ʻo Halemaʻumaʻu ma Kīlauea, ma ka Pāka Aupuni ʻo Kīlauea. ʻO ia ka home o Pele, ke akua Hawaiʻi o ke ahi.





Samuel Kamakau

He poʻe Hawaiʻi ʻo Samuel Manaiakalani Kamakau (29 ʻOkakopa 1815 – 5 Kepakemapa 1876). He poʻe kākau moʻolelo ʻo ia a he mea ʻimi naʻauao ʻo ia.
Hea inoa ʻia ʻo Ke Kula ʻo Samuel M. Kamakau no kēia kanaka.
Kona ola.
Ua hānau ʻia ʻo Kamakau ma Mokulēʻia, Hawaiʻi. Ua hele ʻo ia i ke kula o Lahainaluna Seminary ma 1833. He haumana ʻo ia o Kahu Sheldon Dibble. Ua male ʻo Kamakau iā S. Hainakolo a ua neʻe lāua i Kīpahulu; ʻo Kīpahulu ka home o kā Kamakau wahine. Ma hope o ka hānau ʻana o kā lāua kaikamahine, ʻo Kukelani Kaʻaʻapookalani, ma Kēkēmapa 1862, ua neʻe lākou i Oʻahu.
Mai 1866 i 1871, ua kākau ʻo Kamakau i ʻekolu mau mahele e pili ana i ka moʻomeheu Hawaiʻi a me nā moʻolelo Hawaiʻi. Ua kākau ʻo ia no nā nūpepa ʻo "Ke Au ʻOkoʻa" a me "Ka Nūpepa Kūʻokoʻa". ʻO "Ka Moʻolelo o Kamehameha I", "Ka Moʻolelo o Nā Kamehameha", a me "Ka Moʻolelo Hawaiʻi" nā inoa o kā Kamakau mau mahele.
I ko Kamakau ola, he luna kānāwai ʻo ia ma Wailuku, Maui. He kau kānāwai ʻo ia no ke Aupuni Mōʻī o Hawaiʻi. Ua make ʻo ia ma 1876.





Vanadium

‘O vanadium ke kumumea kemikala iwakāluakūmākolu.





Anne Hathaway

ʻO Anne Hathaway ka inoa o:





Leonardo da Vinci

He polymath ʻĪkālia ʻo Leonardo da Vinci. He kanaka ʻepekema, kanaka makemakika, ʻenekinia, kanaka hakuhia, kanaka ʻanakomia, kaha kiʻi, mea kālai kiʻi, kaha kiʻi hale, kanaka kālailau nahele, mea puolo, a mea kākau ʻo ia.





2009

‘O ka makahiki 2009 (‘elua kaukani ‘ehiku) he makahiki ma‘amau i ho‘omaka ma Pō‘akahi i ka ‘Alemanaka o Kelekolio.
2005 « 2006 « 2007 « 2008 « 2009 





Mauritiusa

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo Mauritiusa (ʻōlelo Palani: "L’île Maurice") kokoke i ka ʻāinapuniʻole ʻo ʻApelika. Aia ʻo ia ma ke komohana hema o ka moana ʻIniana, a he 900 kilomika ko ke kaʻawale ma waena o Mauritiusa a Makakakeka (Madagaseka).
ʻIke ʻia ʻo Mauritiusa no ka dodo. ʻO Mauritiusa ka home wale nō no ka dodo.





A‘ufaga

He kaona li‘ili‘i ‘o A‘ufaga i ka mokupuni ‘o ‘Upolu ma Kāmoa Komohana.





Afega

He kaona li‘ili‘i ‘o Afega i ka mokupuni ‘o ‘Upolu ma Kāmona Komohana.
No Afega kekahi mau ‘ālapa kaulana:





Alafua

He kaona li‘ili‘i ‘o Alafua i ka mokupuni ‘o ‘Upolu ma Kāmoa Komohana. Aia ke Kulanui o ka Pākīpika Hema ma Alafua ma ‘ane‘i.





Aopo

He kaona li‘ili‘i ‘o Aopo i ka mokupuni ‘o Savai‘i ma Kāmoa Komohana.





Apai

He kaona li‘ili‘i ‘o Apai i ka mokupuni ‘o Manono ma Kāmoa Komohana.





Apia

‘O Apia ke kapikala o Kāmoa Komohana. Aia ‘o Apia i ka mokupuni ‘o ‘Upolu.





Kamehameha II

ʻO Kamehameha II (1797 — 14 Iulai 1824) ka mōʻī ʻelua o ke Aupuni Mōʻī o Hawaiʻi. ʻO Kalaninui kua Liholiho i ke kapu ʻIolani kona inoa piha.
Ola ma mua.
Ua hānau ʻia ʻo Liholiho ma Hilo, Hawaiʻi. ʻO Kamehameha I lāua ʻo Keōpūolani nā inoa o kona mau mākua.





Afiamalu

Aia ‘o Afiamalu i ka mokupuni ‘o ‘Upolu ma Kāmona Komohana.





Aiga-i-le-Tai

He moku ‘o Aiga-i-le-Tai o Kāmoa Komohana ma ka mokupuni ‘o ‘Upolu. Aia nā mokupuni li‘ili‘i ‘ekolu ‘o Manono, ‘o Apolima a ‘o Nuulopa kekahi ma ka moku ‘o Aiga-i-le-Tai. ‘O Mulifanua ke kapikala o Aiga-i-le-Tai.





Seine

He kahawai ʻo Seine ma Palani.





Huahine

He mokupuni ‘o Huahine i ka Pae‘āina Polapola ma ka Polenekia Palani.





Manuae

He moku kua‘au ‘o Manuae i ka Pae‘āina Polapola ma ka Polenekia Palani.





Puahōlani

He pua hua kanu ka puahōlani.





Lio

He māmela maiʻao ka lio (inoa Lākina: "Equus caballus") o ka ʻohana kālaimeaola ʻo Equidae.





Pōpoki

He māmela ka pōpoki (inoa Lākina: "Felis catus").





Lāpaki

He māmela iki ka lāpaki o ka ʻohana kālaimeaola ʻo Leporidae.





ʻAnekelopa

He māmela ka ʻanekelopa i ka ʻohana kālaimeaola ʻo Bovidae.





Māhele:Honolulu

ʻO Honolulu ke kapikala o Hawaiʻi.





Akeakamai

He huaʻōlelo ʻo akeakamai a i ʻole ʻepekema e pili ana i nā ʻōnaehana ʻike.





Pauka niho

He palaholo ka pauka niho no ka hoʻomaʻemaʻe ʻana a me ka mālama ʻana i nā niho.





Nainoa Thompson

He hoʻokele Hawaiʻi ʻo Nainoa Thompson. ʻO ia ka luna hoʻokō o Polynesian Voyaging Society.





Moku‘āina

He wahi ka mokuʻāina me ka launa ʻana.





Māhele:Disambig

He papa kēia ʻaoʻao huaʻōlelo puana like o nā mea me ka inoa like.





Mīkini helu

He maomeka ka mīkini helu no ka hoʻomaulia ʻana o nā haʻihelu makemakika.





Palapola

I ka makemakika, he māhele ʻōpuʻu ka palapola.





2008

‘O ka makahiki 2008 (‘elua kaukani ‘ehiku) he makahiki ma‘amau i ho‘omaka ma Pō‘akahi i ka ‘Alemanaka o Kelekolio.

Burakina Faso

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo Burakina Faso ma ʻApelika Komohana. ʻO Ouagadougou ke kapikala o Burakina Faso.





Gāna

He kaumokuʻāina ʻo Gāna ma ʻApelika Komohana.





Pai (makemakika)

I ka makemakika, ʻo pai a i ʻole π ka lākiō o ke anapuni o kekahi pōʻai i ke anawaena o ka pōʻai. He helu hoʻohana ʻo ia, a ʻo ia ka lākiō o ko kekahi pōʻai ʻalea i ka pāhoʻonui lua o kahahānai o ka pōʻai. ʻO ka waiwai helu o π kokoke i 3.14159. Nui nā hana no π i ka makemakika, ke akeakamai, a me ka wilikī.
Nā ʻike kumu.
Ka huaʻōlelo π.
He huaʻōlelo Helene ʻo pai. ʻO "pi" ke kepela ʻana i ka ʻōlelo Helene. ʻAʻole hoʻomaʻaka (∏) ʻo pai ma ka hoʻomaka ʻana o kekahi hopunaʻōlelo ma ka makemakika a me ka ʻepekema. I ka ʻōlelo Helene, ʻo /pi/ ka puana ʻana o pai. Kokoke ka puana ʻana Hawaiʻi o π i ka puana ʻana Pelekane.
Kapa ʻia kēia helu hoʻohana i "π" no ka mea ʻo "π" ka huapalapala mua loa o ka huaʻōlelo Helene ʻo περίμετρος (anapuni).
Ka wehewehe ʻana.
I ke anahonua Euclid, ʻo π ka lākiō o ke anapuni i ke anawaena o ka pōʻai.





Helu piha

ʻO nā helu piha nā hua helu kumu me ka helu 0 (1, 2, 3, ...) a me nā helu piha ʻiʻo ʻole (0, -1, -2, -3, ...). Nā laʻana: he mau helu piha nā helu 65, 7, a me -756; ʻaʻole nā helu 1.6 a me 1½ he mau helu piha.





Helu kumu

ʻO nā helu kumu nā hua helu kumu me nā helu komo mōakaaka: ʻekahi (1) a me ia helu. ʻO nā helu kumu iwakāluakūmālima mua:





‘Ōlelo Ekepelānako

‘O ka ‘ōlelo Ekepelānako (ai‘ole "Esperanto") kekahi ‘ōlelo i ho‘ohana nui ‘ia e nā kānaka a puni ke ao. Ua hana ‘o Lukuiki Lakalo Kamenahopa ka ‘ōlelo o nā ʻāina ʻē. Ma kahi o 100,000-2 miliona ka nui o nā po‘e e ‘ōlelo ana i ka ‘ōlelo Ekepelānako ma ke ‘ano he ‘ōlelo mua.





Brigitte Bardot

‘O Brigitte Bardot (hānau ‘ia ma 28 Kekemapa 1934) kekahi wahine hana keaka Palani, kekahi mea paikini, kekahi pu‘ukani, ame kekahi mea hoʻouluulu no nā pono o nā holoholona.





Sarah Bernhardt

‘O Sarah Bernhardt (22 ‘Okakopa 1844 – 26 Malaki 1923) kekahi wahine hana keaka Palani, ame kapa ‘ia ‘oia, "ka wahine hana keaka kaulana loa ma ka mo‘olelo o ka honua".





Marlon Brando

‘O Marlon Brando, Jr. (3 ‘Apelila 1924 – 1 Iulai 2004) kekahi mea hana keaka i lanakila ai i nā Academy Award. Mana‘o nā po‘e, ‘o ia kekahi mea hana keaka nui loa ma ka honua.





‘Ōlelo Pākē

‘O ka ‘ōlelo Pākē kekahi ‘ohana ‘ōlelo, a he mau ‘ōlelo kona mai ka ‘āina Pākē.





Wakinekona, D.C.

ʻO Wakinekona, D.C. ("Wakinekona Dēsē"; i ka ʻōlelo Pelekane, "Washington, D.C."), kapa paʻalula ʻia ʻo District of Columbia ("ʻĀpana o Kolumepia") ke kapikala o ʻAmelika Hui Pū ʻia.





Moanalua

He kaiahome ʻo Moanalua ma Honolulu, Hawaiʻi.





Māhele:Aliʻi o Hawaiʻi

Eia nā aliʻi o Hawaiʻi mai ke aupuni mōʻī o Hawaiʻi.





Wikipedia:Palapala ho‘okuleana

formula_1





Aupuni Mōʻī o Hawaiʻi

He aupuni mōʻī ke Aupuni Mōʻī o Hawaiʻi. Ua hoʻokumu ʻo ia ma waena o nā makahiki 1795-1810.





Đồng Hới

ʻO Đồng Hới ke kapikala o ka panalā‘au o Quảng Binh i Wiekanama.





Lōʻihi

ʻO Lōʻihi he mauna kai a he lua pele lalo kai ma kahi o 48 klm (30 mil) ma ka hikina hema o ka moku ʻo Hawaiʻi. Aia ʻo Lōʻihi ma ka ʻaoʻao o Mauna Loa, ka lua pele kuahene nui loa i ka honua. ʻO Lōʻihi ka lua pele hou loa i ka pae mauna kai ʻo Hawaiʻi-ʻEmepela. ʻAʻole like ʻo Lōʻihi me nā lua pele ma ka lei o Pele. Ua hoʻokumu ʻo Lōʻihi ma ka piko pele Hawaiʻi. E hoʻopuka paha ana ʻo Lōʻihi ma luna o nā nalu i 10,000—100,000 makahiki mua aku.





Jonathan Nāpela

ʻO Jonathan Nāpela (1813–1879; kapa ʻia ʻo Jonatana a i ʻole Iohatana Hawaiʻi Nāpelakapuonamahanaonāleleonālani) he lālā o ka Hoʻomana o Iesu Kristo o nā Poʻe Hoʻāno o nā Lā Hope Nei. Ua huli ʻo ia ma mua o ka hapa nui o nā poʻe. Na Nāpela lāua ʻo George Q. Cannon i unuhi i ka Puke o Molemona i ka ʻōlelo Hawaiʻi. Ua hele ʻo ia i ke Kula ʻo Lahainaluna.
He luna kānāwai ʻo Napela i ka manawa o kona hui ʻana me Cannon. Ma hope o kona huli ʻana i ka Hoʻomana o Iesu Kristo o nā Poʻe Hoʻāno o nā Lā Hope Nei, ʻaʻole ʻo ia he luna kānāwai.
Kapa ʻia ka Hawaiian Studies Center ma ke Kulanui ʻo Brigham Young iā Nāpela.





Mauna kai

ʻO ka mauna kai he mauna ma lalo o ka ʻilikai. No laila, ʻaʻole ka mauna kai he mokupuni.





Wā Classical

A' aweeki malooki aweanamonapia





Hunaola

‘O ka hunaola ka māhele iki loa o ke ola.





Matsuo Bashō

‘O Matsuo Bashō (松尾 芭蕉, 1644 – 28 Nowemapa 1694) kekahi haku mele kaulana loa o ka wā Edo ma Iāpana.





Māhele:Kahaki‘i

Eia nā kahaki‘i.





Vincent van Gogh

‘O Vincent Willem van Gogh (30 Malaki 1853 – 29 Iulai 1890) kekahi kahaki‘i Hōlani. Kahaki‘i ‘oia i ke ‘ano Post-Impressionism.





Michelangelo

‘O Michelangelo di Lodovico Buonarroti Simoni (6 Malaki 1475 – 18 Pepeluali 1564), ai‘ole Michelangelo, kekahi kahaki‘i, mea kālai kiʻi, kaha kiʻi hale, haku mele ame wilikī Ikalia o ka wā Renaissance.

Paipala

ʻO ka Paipala a i ʻole ka Baibala ka puke kapu o ka Hoʻomana Iukaio a me ka Hoʻomana Kalikiano.





Qin Shi Huang

‘O Qin Shi Huang (秦始皇,259 BCE – 210 BCE) kekahi Caiser o ka wā Qin.

Mauna Kana Helena

He luapele ʻo Mauna Kana Helena ma ke Kalana ʻo Skamania, Wakinekona, ma ke komohana ʻākau o ʻAmelika Hui Pū ʻia. Aia ʻo ia ma ka hema o Seattle a me ka hikina ʻākau o Portland, ʻOlekona.

Knoxville, Kenekī

ʻO Knoxville ka ʻekolu kūlanakauhale nui o Kenekī, ma hope o Memapika a me Nakawila, a me ka noho kalana o ke Kalana o Knox.





Houston, Kekeka

ʻO Houston ke kūlanakauhale nui ʻehā o ʻAmelika Hui Pū ʻia a me ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o Kekeka.





Kikako, ʻIlinoe

ʻO Kikako ke kūlanakauhale nui ʻekolu o ʻAmelika Hui Pū ʻia a me ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o ʻIlinoe.

Maracena

Musée d'Orsay

O ka Hale Hō‘ike‘ike o Orsay (‘ōlelo Palani: Musée d'Orsay) ka hale hō‘ike‘ike hana no‘eau i kipa ‘ia nui loa, he pāka kiaho‘omana‘o aupuni, ame he hō‘ailona aupuni. Aia ka hale hō‘ike‘ike ma Palika, Palani.
<br clear="all">





Kaulana Nā Pua

He mele Hawaiʻi ʻo Kaulana Nā Pua i haku mele ʻia na Ellen Kehoʻohiwaokalani Wright Prendergast i ka makahiki 1893 no ke kūʻē ʻana o ko Liliʻuokalani hoʻokahuli ʻia ʻana.





Nepekune

‘O Nepekune ka hōkū hele ‘ewalu mai ka Lā ma ke kahua o nā hōkū.





Kauoha Hou

ʻO ke Kauoha Hou (ʻōlelo Helene: Καινὴ Διαθήκη) ka paukū lua o ka Paipala Hemolele, lāua pū me ke Kauoha Kahiko.





Makua Kamiano

He kahu Kākolika Loma ʻo Kāna Kamiano ka Pōmaikaʻi o Molokaʻi (3 Ianuali 1840 – 15 ʻApelila 1889), kapa ʻia ʻo Jozef De Veuster ma kona hānau ʻia ʻana, a kapa ʻia ʻo Damien De Veuster nō hoʻi (ʻōlelo Hōlani: "Pater Damiaan" a i ʻole "Zalige Damiaan De Veuster"). No Pelekiuma mai ʻo ia. Ua lilo ʻo ia i kāna ma 11 ʻOkakopa 2009. Kaulana ʻo ia ma muli o kona kōkua ʻana i nā poʻe me ka maʻi lēpela ma Kalaupapa.





Sila Hawaiʻi

He sila ʻane halapohe ka Sila Hawaiʻi ("Monachus schauinslandi"), kapa ʻia ʻīlio-holo-i-ka-uaua. ʻĀpaʻakuma kēia sila i nā wai a puni i nā moku Hawaiʻi.





Jonah Kūhiō Kalanianaʻole

He keiki aliʻi ʻo Jonah Kūhiō Kalanianaʻole (26 Malaki 1871 – 7 Ianuali 1922) o ka Hale o Kalākaua ma ka hoʻokahuli ʻia ʻana o ke Aupuni Mōʻī ʻo Hawaiʻi. ʻO David Kawānanakoa lāua ʻo Edward Abner Keliʻiahonui kona mau kaikuaʻana.
Kona wā liʻiliʻi.
Ua hānau ʻia ʻo Jonah Kūhiō Kalanianaʻole ma Kōloa, Kauaʻi ma ka lā 26 Malaki 1871. Ua hea inoa ʻia ʻo ia no kona mau kupuna kāne, ʻo Kūhiō Kalanianaʻole, ke aliʻi o Hilo, lāua ʻo Jonah Piʻikoi, ke aliʻi o Kauaʻi. Ua hele ʻo ia i ke Kula ʻo Royal a me ke Kula ʻo Punahou. Ma hope o kona aʻo ʻana ma Hawaiʻi, ua hele ʻo ia i ke Kulanui o St. Matthews ma Kaleponi a me ke Kulanui ʻo Royal Agricultural ma ʻEnelani.





Kōlea ʻĀkau

He ʻāina ʻo Kōlea ʻĀkau (inoa kūhelu: Lepupalika Kemokalaka ʻo Kōlea o nā Kānaka; ʻōlelo Kōlea: 조선민주주의인민공화국) ma ka ʻAnemoku ʻo Kōlea ma ka hikina o ʻĀkia. ʻO Pyongyang kona kapikala a me kona kūlanakauhale nui loa.





George Nāʻope

He kumu hula ʻo George Lanakilakekiahialiʻi Nāʻope (25 Pepeluali 1928 — 26 ʻOkakopa 2009). Nāna i aʻo aku i ka hula no kanaono makahiki ma Hawaiʻi, Guama, ʻAukekulelia, Kelemānia, ʻEnelani, a me nā ʻāinapuniʻole ʻo ʻAmelika ʻĀkau lāua ʻo ʻAmelika Hema.
Ma hope o ko Nāʻope hānau ʻia ʻana ma Kalihi, Hawaiʻi, ua aʻo mai ʻo ia i ka hula mai kona kupuna wahine kuakahi, ʻo Mary Malia Pukaokalani Nāʻope, ma kona makahiki ʻekolu. I kona makahiki ʻehā, ua aʻo mai ʻo ia me Mary Kanaele, ka makuahine o Edith Kanakaʻole.
I ka makahiki 1964, ua hoʻokumu ʻo Nāʻope i ka hoʻolauleʻa ʻo Mele Manaka.
Ua hala ʻo Nāʻope ma ka lā 26 ʻOkakopa 2009 ma Hilo, Hawaiʻi.





Kalikimaka

He lānui makahiki ʻo Kalikimaka ma Kēkēmapa 25. Hoʻomanaʻo ʻia ka hānau ʻia ʻana o Iesū ma kēia lā. ʻAʻole i ʻike ʻia ka lā maoli o ko Iesū lā hānau. Ua koho paha kēia lā no kekahi hoʻolauleʻa Loma a i ʻole ka māuikiʻikiʻi o ka hoʻoilo.





Heleuī

He lānui makahiki ʻo Heleuī ma ʻOkakopa 31.





Isaac Newton

He kanaka koʻikoʻi ʻo Isaac Newton mai Pelekāne. He mea kālaikūlohea, he mea makemakika, a he mea aʻo hōkū ʻo ia. Koʻikoʻi paha kona puke, ʻo "Philosophiæ Naturalis Principia Mathematica" (kapa pinepine ʻia ʻo "Principia") nō hoʻi, i paʻi ʻia ma ka makahiki 1687.





Kaʻiulani

ʻO Victoria Kaʻiulani Kalaninuiahilapalapa Kawēkiu i Lunalilo Cleghorn (16 ʻOkakopa 1875 – 6 Malaki 1899) ka hoʻoilina mōʻī wahine hope loa o ke Aupuni Mōʻī Hawaiʻi. Ma hope o ka hoʻokahuli ʻia ʻana o ke Aupuni Mōʻī i ka makahiki 1893, ua alakaʻi ʻo ia i ka paipai kālaiʻāina no ka hoʻihoʻi ea o ke Aupuni.
Kona wā liʻiliʻi.
Ua hānau ʻia ʻo Kaʻiulani ma Honolulu. ʻO Miriam Likelike kona makuahine, a he moʻopuna kuakahi ʻo Likelike o Kepoʻokalani, kekahi hoa hānau o Kamehameha I. ʻO Archibald Cleghorn, kekahi pāʻoihana Kekokia, kona makuakāne.





Likelike

He kamāliʻi wahine ʻo Miriam Kapili Kekauluohi Likelike (13 Ianuali 1851 – 2 Pepeluali 1887) o ke Aupuni Mōʻī Hawaiʻi.
Kona ola.
ʻO Miriam Likelike ke kaikamahine muli loa o Caesar Kapaʻakea lāua ʻo Analea Keohokālole. ʻO ia ka pōkiʻi o Moses Kapaʻakea, James Kaliokalani, David Kalākaua, Lydia Liliʻuokalani, Kaiminaʻauao, a me Anna Kaʻiulani. ʻO ia ka hānau mua o Leleiohōkū II.
Ua male ʻo Likelike iā Archibald Cleghorn ma ka lā 22 Kepakemapa 1870. Ua hānau ʻo ia iā Kaʻiulani ma ka lā 16 ʻOkakopa 1875.
Ua hāʻule ʻo Likelike ma ka lā 2 Pepeluali 1887. ʻAʻole ʻike ʻia ke kumu o kona hāʻule ʻana; ua hōʻole paha ʻo ia i nā meaʻai a pau.





Māhele:Hawaiʻi

Eia nā mea e pili ana iā Hawaiʻi, ka mokuʻāina kanalima o ʻAmelika Hui Pū ʻia.





Heiti

He ʻāina ʻo Heiti (ʻōlelo Palani: "Haïti"), kapa kūhelu ʻia ʻo ka Lepupalika ʻo Heiti ("République d'Haïti") ma ke Kalepiana. Aia pū ʻo Heiti me ka Lepupalika ʻo Kominika ma ka mokupuni ʻo Hispaniola.





Māhele:Kapikala o nā mokuʻāina o ʻAmelika Hui

Eia nā kapikala o nā mokuʻāina o ʻAmelika Hui Pū ʻia.





Kelewikiona

‘O Kelewikiona ke ʻōnaehana pūnaewele nona ho’olele leo a kipa ‘ana o ne’ena ki’i a leo mōʻiu.





Ka'aahi Thomas

‘O Ka’aahi Thomas ("Thomas the Tank Engine and Friends") ke pūkaʻina polokalamu kīwī no kamali’i kumu i "The Railway Series" hana e ke Rev. W. Awdry. Ka polokalamu ua i kona mua hi’ona i 1984. Ringo Starr ua ka mua haʻi moʻolelo o nā pūkaʻina polokalamu kīwī.





'Imi loa Dora

‘O ‘Imi loa Dora ("Dora the Explorer") ke pūkaʻina polokalamu kīwī no kamali’i pēlā ho’olaha i Nickelodeon i ka ‘Amelika Hui Pū ‘ia. La kuhina nui i 2000.





Backyardigans

`O Backyardigans ke 3D CGI hō`eleu pūka`ina polokalamu kīwī ua nāmua la Nick Jr. i 2004.





Teletubbies

‘O Teletubbies ke pūkaʻina polokalamu kīwī no kamali’i ho`ohua i ka Aupuni Mōʻī Hui Pū ʻia. La kuhina nui i 1997.





Pelanekelina

`O Pelanekelina ("Franklin") ke pūkaʻina polokalamu kīwī no kamali’i ho`ohua no Kanakā, hana e mahele o puke e Brenda Clark a Paulette Bourgeois. La kuhina nui i 1997.





Māhele:Kapikala o ʻAmelika Hui






Johannes Vermeer

‘O Johannes Vermeer (31 Okakopa 1632 – 15 Kēkēmapa 1675) kekahi kahaki‘i Hōlani. Kahaki‘i ‘oia i ke ‘ano Baroque.





Georges de La Tour

‘O Georges de La Tour (13 Malaki 1593 – 30 Ianuari 1652) kekahi kahaki‘i Palani. Kahaki‘i ‘oia i ke ‘ano Baroque.





Nikolai Rimsky-Korsakov

He haku mele ‘o Nikolai Andreyevich Rimsky-Korsakov (1844-1908). Ua hānau ʻia ʻo Rimsky-Korsakov ma Tikhvin Rūsia.





John Singer Sargent

‘O John Singer Sargent (12 Ianuali 1856 – 15 ‘Apelila 1925) kekahi kahaki‘i ‘Amelika Hui Pū ‘ia . 





Hoʻomana Buda

ʻO Siddhartha Gautama ka inoa o ka mea i kapa ʻia ʻo Buda i kēia manawa. Ua lele a mahae kēia hoʻomana mai ʻĪnia aku. He aliʻi ʻo Siddhatha Gautama i milimili a aloha nui ʻia e kona mākua. ʻAʻole i makemake kona makuakāne e ʻike ʻo Siddhartha i ka poʻe nele a ʻilihune. No laila ʻo ia i hūnā a alualu ai i ia ʻano poʻe mai Siddhartha aku. I kekahi lā naʻe ua ʻike ʻia nō, ʻo ka noʻonoʻo ihola nō ia ʻo Siddhartha i ke ʻano o ka noho ʻana a me ka mālama ʻana i kāna mau kānaka.





Ivan Shishkin

‘O Ivan Ivanovich Shishkin (25 Ianuari 1832 – 20 Malaki 1898) kekahi kahaki‘i Rūsia. 





Ivan Kramskoi

‘O Ivan Nikolaevich Kramskoi (1837 – 1887) kekahi kahaki‘i Rūsia. 





Kālaiʻāina

ʻO ke kālaiʻāina he huaʻōlelo kahiko kēia no ka hana a ke aupuni, ʻo ia hoʻi ka ʻaoʻao politika ma kēia wā. Nui ʻino nā ʻano o nā aupuni o nēia wā a me ka wā i hala.





Maki a Ruby

‘O Maki a Ruby ("Max and Ruby") ke pūkaʻina polokalamu kīwī nāna kamali’i, kumu i na puke nana Rosemary Wells. Ka polokalamu ua i kona mua hi’ona i 2002.





Rembrandt

O Rembrandt Harmenszoon van Rijn (15 Iulai 1606 – 4 Okakopa 1669) kekahi kahaki‘i Hōlani. Kahaki‘i ‘oia i ke ‘ano Baroque.





Sesame Street

‘O Sesame Street ke ‘Amelika Hui Pū ‘ia polokalamu kīwī no kamali’i kēlā maka mua puka i Nowemapa 10, 1969.





Sandy Beach

Me kahakai one ‘o ke‘oke‘o wai milimili uliuli.





Care Bears

ʻO Care Bears ke pūkaʻina polokalamu kīwī a ‘Amelika kahahiō o mea pāʻani ka i ua makemake nui ʻia hoʻohua nō 1981.

Mölnlycke

Pinnipedia

Waleluka

He māmela o ʻohana waleluka ka waleluka (Lākina: "Odobenus rosmarus").





Canidae

Maupaʻa ka ʻOhana ʻīlio (inoa Lākina: Canidae) i ka ʻīlio kūloko, ke iākala, ka ʻīlio hae, ke kaioke a me ka ʻalopeke.





Felidae

Maupaʻa ka ʻOhana pōpoki (inoa Lākina: Felidae) i ka pōpoki, ka liona, ka leopaki, ka kika (tiga), ka leopaki kikī, ka lineka, ke koukā a me ke iākua.





Otariidae

Maupaʻa ka ʻOhana sila-me-nā-pepeiao (inoa Lākina: Otariidae) i ka liona kai, bea kai a me ka sila pūhuluhulu.





Phocidae

Maupaʻa ka ʻOhana sila kūʻiʻo (inoa Lākina: Phocidae) i ka sila, ka leopaki kai, ka ʻelepani kai a me ka sila Hawaiʻi.





Cervidae

Maupaʻa ka ʻOhana kia (inoa Lākina: Cervidae) i ke kia, ka muniaka, ka pūpalō, ke kia kitala, ka ʻēleka, ka wapiki a me ka leinekia.





ʻOhana pipi

Maupaʻa ka ʻOhana pipi (aiʻole ʻOhana bipi; inoa Lākina: Bovidae) i ka pipi, ka pipi kuapuʻu, ka pāpulō, ka pipi Pākē, ka ʻanekelopa, ke kākela, ka hipa, ke kao a me ke iaka.





Edentata

Maupaʻa ke Kaʻina o māmela niho ʻole (inoa Lākina: Edentata) i ka ʻamakila, ka melalemu, ka panolina, ka tamanua, ʻainaonao a me ka ʻainaonao ʻōlae.





Nalala

Maupaʻa ka "superorder" Nalala (inoa Lākina: Dinosauria) i ka tiranosauru, ka barakiosauru, ka setegasauru, ka terikeratopa, ka peterosauru, ka ʻanekilosauru a me ka welokirapetoa.

Pule






'ōlelo toki pona

He 'ōlelo o ka pono ka 'ōlelo toki pona, e hahai 'oia i ke ola maika'i me ka ma'alahi i ka 'āina. E kau nui ana ka mana'o i nā kumumea pono e ola, ke waiho nei ia i kona iho me he 'ōlelo, penei hiki ke kānaka e a'o iā'oia. He haneri me ka 'umikumamawalu 'ōlelo. No ke aha e kali 'oukou?
