ʻōlelo Helene

Ka ʻōlelo Helene (Helene: ελληνικά) ka ʻōlelo no na ʻāina Helene.





Guiado por Deus, iluminado e protegido pela força de Zeus

Guiado por Deus, iluminado e protegido pela força de Zeus





Rafael Correa

ʻO Rafael Correa (ʻōlelo Hawaiʻi: Rafael Correa) hānau ʻia ma ʻAukake 4, 1963) ka pelekikena o Ecuador i kēia manawa.





ʻAperodite

ʻO ʻAperodite (‘olelo Helene Aφροδίτη, "Afrodítē") ka akua wahine o ke aloha a me ka nani. ʻO ia ka kaikamahine o ʻUlano (like me ʻo Hesioda).





Hesioda

ʻO Hesioda (ʻōlelo Helene Ἡσίοδος, "Hēsíodos" aiʻole Hekioda) ka haku mele mai Helene. Iaia puke ka "Theogonía".
ʻOia haʻi hānau ʻeʻepa o akua wahine ʻAperodite (akua wahine o ke aloha) a me hānau o nā hoa aliʻi. ʻOia ua kaulana.





Likaono

Likaono (ʻōlelo Helene "Λυκαων", "Lykaôn") ka Mōʻī o ʻAkakia i loko Helene. 
Makua kāne o Likaono ua "Πελασγός" (Pelaseguso). Makua wahine o Likaono ua akua wahine Melipoia ("Meliboia").
Likaono loaʻa nui ʻino nā wahine a me nui ʻino nā kama kāne.
Ua i loko hekau lupo.





ʻOeneusa

ʻO ʻOeneusa (ʻōlelo Helene "Οἰνεύς") ka Mōʻī a Kalidono i loko Helene, keiki a Mōʻī Porotaono a me ʻEurite, pilikua o ʻAlataea a me makua kāne a Meleagerosa, Deianira a me Tudeusa.

Lipekika

He kūlanakauhale ʻo Lipekika o Kelemānia. ʻO Leipzig kona inoa Kelemānia. Kaulana kona Hōʻikeʻike pāʻoihana kūmakahiki. Ua hoʻokahua ʻia ke Kulanui o Lipekika i ka makahiki 1409.





Makekepuka

He kūlanakauhale ʻo Makekepuka o Kelemānia. ʻO Magdeburg kona inoa Kelemānia. 231.525 a Makekepuka poʻe.
Ua pau ke kūkulu ʻana i ka Hale Pule Nui Kokika a Makekepuka i ka makahiki 1520.





Hamepuka

He kūlanakauhale nui ʻo Hamepuka o Kelemānia ʻĀkau. ʻO Hamburg kona inoa Kelemānia. Kaulana kona awa nui. 1.802.041 a Hamepuka poʻe.





ʻōhiʻa lomi

He mea kanu ka ʻōhiʻa lomi ("lycopersicon esculentum").





ʻAlepa

He pae mauna nunui a me nā kuahiwi kuahea nā ʻAlepa ma ʻEulopa. ʻO Mont Blanc kona mauna kiʻekiʻe loa.





Johann Wolfgang von Goethe

He haku mele kaulana ʻo Goethe o Kelemānia, o ka wā kelakikala. ʻO Johann Wolfgang von Goethe (puana Kelemānia: [ˈjoːhan ˈvɔlfɡaŋ fɔn ˈɡøːtə]) kona inoa piha. Hānau ʻia ʻo Goethe i ka makahiki 1749, ma ka lā 28 ʻAukake, ma Palanipoka (ma ka ʻōlelo Kelemānia, Frankfurt am Main). Nui loa kāna hana hihiu. Kaulana kāna keaka hopena kaumaha "Faust".
Make ‘o Johann Wolfgang von Goethe ma ka lā 22 Malaki 1832 ma Wehimala (ma ka ʻōlelo Kelemānia, Weimar).





Friedrich Schiller

He haku mele kaulana ʻo Schiller o Kelemānia, o ka wā kelakikala. ʻO Johann Christoph Friedrich von Schiller (puana Kelemānia: [ˈjoːhan ˈkʁɪstɔf ˈfʁiːdʁɪç fɔn ˈʃɪlɐ]) kona inoa piha. Hānau ʻia ʻo Schiller ma ka lā 10 Nowemapa 1759 ma Marbach am Neckar. Nui loa kāna hana hihiu. Kaulana kāna hana keaka ʻekahi "Die Räuber" (ma ka ʻōlelo Hawaiʻi, "Nā ʻAihue"), ā nui kāna mau hana keaka ʻē aʻe a me kāna mau mele. Noho ʻo ia ma Wehimala (ma ka ʻōlelo Kelemānia, Weimar). Aia ʻo Goethe, kona hoa pili, i laila i ka manawa hoʻokahi.
Make ‘o Schiller ma ka lā 09 Mei 1805 ma Wehimala.





Wehimala

He kūlanakauhale liʻiliʻi ʻo Wehimala i Tulinia. ʻO Weimar kona inoa Kelemānia.





Tulinia

He mokuʻāina ʻo Tulinia o Kelemānia. ʻO Thüringen kona inoa Kelemānia (ma ka ʻōlelo Pelekānia, Thuringia).





Haukapila ʻo Kapiʻolani

ʻO ka haukapila ʻo Kapiʻolani kekahi o nā haukapila o Hawaiʻi Pacific Health ma Makiki, Oʻahu, Hawaiʻi. Ua hoʻokahua ʻia kēia haukapila e Kapiʻolani i ka makahiki 1890 me ka inoa ʻo "Kapiʻolani Maternity Home". ʻO kēia haukapila ka wahi hānau o Barack Obama, ka pelekikena kanahākūmāhā o ʻAmelika Hui Pū ʻia.





Velasquita Ramírez

Velasquita Ramírez (‘Ōlelo Hawai‘i: Welasikita Ramirez aiʻole Welakikika Lamileka) (? - 1036) ka kuini o León ma Sepania.
Kāna kāne ka Bermudo II o León.
Kaikamahine o Velasquita ka kamāliʻi wahine Cristina Bermúdez.
Makua kāne o Velasquita malia paha ka Ramiro Menéndez.





Úrsula Murayama

ʻO Úrsula Murayama (‘Ōlelo Hawai‘i: Ulukula Mulaiama) ka wahine hana keaka mai Mekiko. ʻOia loaʻa welo Kepanī ā noho i Sepania.
Kāna kūkū kāne aiʻole makua kāne ua mea hana keaka Noé Murayama.
Hānau ʻia ʻo Úrsula ma Mekiko.
Nā hāmeʻe a Úrsula: 





Kamehameha III

Kamehameha III (hānau Kauikeaouli) (1813-1854) ua ka mōʻī o Hawaiʻi mai 1825 i 1854. Kona piha inoa Keaweaweʻula Kīwalaʻō Kauikeaouli Kaleiopapa ā laila hoʻolōʻihi nō Kauikeaouli Kaleiopapa and then lengthened to Keaweaweʻula Kīwalaʻō Kauikeaouli Kaleiopapa Kalani Waiakua Kalanikau Iokikilo Kīwalaʻō i ke kapu Kamehameha i ʻo ia hoʻoaliʻi ka mea mōʻī.
Ua loli Hawaiʻi mai he piha aupuni mōʻī i he aupuni mōʻī kū i ke kumukānāwai Kalikiano a me ka hōʻailona ʻo lāua ʻelua 1840 kumukānāwai a me 1852 kumukānāwai, malalo kona noho aliʻi. Ua noho aliʻi nō 29 makahiki a me 192 lā, ʻoiai i ka mahele mua o kona noho aliʻi i lalo ka noho aliʻi na Kuini Kaʻahumanu ā mahope aku na Kuini Kaʻahumanu II, ʻo ia ka mōʻī noho aliʻi loa nui. Kona kumu hoʻokaulike akahele o hoʻonupaikini i ʻāpono nā ʻano haole, i ka manawa mālama kona aupuni pū.
Ola Kama.
Ua hānau Kauikeaouli i Keauhou, i Hawaiʻi, ka moku nui loa i kō Hawaiʻi pae ʻāina. ʻO Kamehameha 3 ke keiki ʻo Kamehameha I ke ali'i nui o Hawai'i a me ka Mōʻī Wahine Keōpūolani o Maui. Ke ʻike ʻole ʻia nei kona miomio lā hānau. Ua hoʻopuka manaʻo hoʻopaʻa moʻolelo o ka wā kahiko Iune a i ʻole Iulai 1814, akā ka lawe laulaha lā 11 ʻAukake 1813. Ua ʻo ia o ke kūʻauhau kapu kiʻekiʻe. Ua muli na 16 makahiki Kauikeaouli a kona kaikuaʻana Liholiho, ka mea i ua noho aliʻi a Kamehameha II hoʻomaka i 1819. Ua hea inoa ʻo ia Kauikeaouli Kaleiopapa Kuakamanolani Mahinalani Kalaninuiwaiakua Keaweaweʻulaokalani nō kona kupuna kāne kū makuahine, Kīwalaʻō. Ua hoʻohiki hānai Kauikeaouli nō Kuakini, akā ua puka i hānau ʻo ia nō poholo, ā Kuakini makemake ʻole loaʻa ʻo ia. Akā ua kāhea Aliʻi Kaikeoʻewa kona kuala, Kapihe ā haʻi ka pēpē ola. Ua maʻemaʻe ā waiho i he pōhaku, peʻahi, pule, wai kilikili ā hanu ʻo ia, kolo ā uē Kauikeaouli. Ka pule o Kapihe nō Kaʻōnohiokalā, “Kama o Akua.” Mālama ka pōhaku me he kia hoʻomanaʻo i Keauhou. Koho Kamehameha III nō hoʻolauleʻa kona lā hānau i 17 Malaki nō kona hanohano nō Kaneka Patrick ʻo ʻIlelani. Ua hāʻawi ʻo ia i Kaikioʻewa i hānai.

La mujer dorada

La mujer dorada (‘Ōlelo Hawai‘i "Ka wahine kula") ka pūkaʻina polokalamu kīwī mai Mekiko. Ia pūkaʻina polokalamu kīwī ʻaʻohe hoʻāpono ma ka anaina.
Pākahi mokuna ua lōʻihi 30 nā minuke.
I loko neia pūkaʻina polokalamu kīwī hoʻomāʻike ka malaka wahine, e ka onaona. Pūkaʻina polokalamu kīwī ka hilu no ko nā peke eia hoʻi nā kāhuli.

Pedro de Betancur

He kahu Kākolika Loma ʻo Santo Hermano Pedro de San José Betancur (21 Malaki 1626 – 25 ʻApelila 1667). No Tenerife (Nā Moku Manu Mele, Sepania) mai ʻo ia, mikanele no Guatemala. Ua lilo ʻo ia i kāna ma 30 ʻIulai 2002. 





ʻŌlelo ʻĪkālia

ʻO ka ʻōlelo ʻĪkālia (i ka ʻōlelo Italia: "lingua italiana" a iʻole "italiano") ka ʻōlelo makuahine o ʻĪkālia.
Piliʻōlelo.
ʻO "kumuhaʻi-haʻina-mea" ka huipaʻa o ka ʻōlelo ʻĪkālia
Hoʻohālikelike:
He kanaka au "io sono un uomo"
Hele ʻoe i ke kula "(tu) andavi a scuola"
Pilimua
ʻO "il, lo, la, gli, le" nā pīlimua.
Il: ke/ka
Lo: ke/ka
La: ke/ka
Gli, le: nā
Ke kanaka "L'uomo" (il/lo + uomo)
Nā kānaka "gli uomini"
ʻAna o nā haʻina.
Hele "Andare"
(Ua) Hele
Ā laila e ho’omau ’oukou pēiā me: "egli andava, noi andavamo, voi andavate, essi andavano"
(E) Hele
Ā laila e ho’omau ’oukou pēiā me: "tu andrai, egli andrà, noi andremo, voi andrete, essi andranno"





Tolstoi

He haku mele kaulana loa ʻo Tolstoi o Lūkia, o ke kenekulia ʻumi kūmāiwa a me ke kenekulia iwakālua. ʻO Lev Nikolayevich Tolstoi kona inoa piha (puana Lūkia [lʲɛf nʲɪkɐˈlaɪvʲɪtɕ tɐlˈstoj], ma ka ʻōlelo Lūkia, Лев Николаевич Толстой). Hānau ʻia ʻo Tolstoi i ka makahiki 1828, ma ka lā 9 Kepakemapa (ma ka lā 28 ʻAukake, mamuli o ka ʻalemanaka Iuliani), ma ke kuleana o kona ʻohana, ʻo Yasnaya Polyana (ma ka ʻōlelo Lūkia, Ясная Поляна). Nui loa kāna hana hihiu. Kaulana kāna mau nōwela "Anna Kalenina" (Анна Каренина, Anna Karenina) a me "Ke kaua a me ka maluhia" (Война и Мир, War and Peace). He ʻano nui kāna nōwela "Ala hou" (Воскресение, Resurrection).
Ua make ʻo Tolstoi ma ka lā 20 Nowemapa 1910 (ma ka lā 7 Nowemapa 1910, mamuli o ka ʻalemanaka Iuliani) ma ka hale hoʻolulu kaʻaahi ʻo Astapovo (ma ka ʻōlelo Lūkia, Астапово).

Sung Jae-gi

Sung Jae-gi (ma ka ʻōlelo Korea:성재기, 成在基), He haku mele kaulana ʻo Sung o South Korea, o ka wā Human right activists ame liberalism Philosophers. ʻO Sung Jae-gi kona inoa piha. Hānau ʻia ʻo Sung i ka makahiki 1967, ma ka lā 11 ʻKepakemapa, ma Daegu (ma ka ʻōlelo Korea, 대구). Nui loa anti feminism movement and liberalism movement hana o South Korea hihiu. ma ka lā Ianuali 24 2008, piholo o Association o Korean kāne(ma ka ʻōlelo South Korea:남성연대, 男性連帶).
ia ō human rights movement ame Masculism movement, South Korean liberalism movement mai 2001–2013.
Make‘o suicide o Sung Jae-gi, ma ka lā Iulai 26 2013 ma Mapo bridge (ma ka ʻōlelo Korea 마포대교), Seoul (ma ka ʻōlelo Korea, 서울). ia ō ka wā hope‘ōlelo, "kāne ō 'ekahi kanaka!(ma ka ʻōlelo Korea 남자도 사람이다!)"

Nā Leokanipū Hāʻukēʻukē

Hoʻohanaʻia nā leokanipū hāʻukēʻukē i nā ʻōlelo Khoisan, ma ʻApelika. ʻO Damin ka ʻōlelo wale nō e hoʻohana i kēia mau leokanipū mawaho o ʻApelika, ma ʻAukekulelia. Kaulana nui kēia mau ʻōlelo mamuli o ke kiʻiʻoniʻoni ʻo "The Gods Must Be Crazy". 
Hoʻohanaʻia lākou i ka ʻŌlelo juǀ'hoan, i ka ʻŌlelo !Xoo, i ka ʻŌlelo Xhosa ā kekahi mau.
ʻO ʘ, ǀ, ǀǀ, ǃ ā me ǂ nā hāʻukēʻukē ʻikeʻia loa.
Hoʻohanaʻia ʘ i nā ʻōlelo !Xoo, ǂHoan ā me Damin wale nō. Kākauʻia ǀ, ǀǀ, ā ! e like me c, x ā q i nā ʻōlelo Xhosa, Zulu ā me Ndebele.

Yun Hyon-seok

He haku mele kaulana ʻo Yun Hyon-seok(윤현석;尹賢碩, ʻAukake 7 1984 - ʻApelila 26 2003) o South Korea, o ka wā Human right activists ame Civil activists, haku poema, kākau. ʻO Yun Hyon-seok(puana Kelemānia: [Yun Hyŏn-sŏk]) kona inoa piha, Yook Woo-dang(육우당;六友堂), Seolheon(설헌;雪軒), Midong(미동;美童) kona nickname piha. Hānau ʻia ʻo Yun i ka makahiki 1984, ma ka lā ʻAukake 7, ma Byupyong(부평;富平, ma ka ʻōlelo South Korea, Incheon).
In 2002 to 2003, he was LGBT Human right activity, In 2003, he was Conscientious objection(양심적 병역 거부) wehewehe. Nui loa kāna hana hihiu, Human right activity culture South Korea, Kaulana kāna keaka hopena kaumaha "My Soul was changed to flower rain(내 영혼은 꽃비 되어)". 
Make‘o suicide o Yun, ma ka lā ʻApelila 26 2003 ma Dongdaemun(동대문;東大門), Seoul. ia ō ka wā Protest of South Korean Homo-phobia.





Keokola Palaiologina Synadene

Keokola Palaiologina Synadene (Helene: "Θεοδώρα Παλαιολογίνα Συναδηνή") ka Helene aliʻi.
Kona makuahine ka Irene Komnene Laskarina Branaina, ʻoiai kona makuakāne ka Konstantinos Palaiologos (aliʻi).
Kaikaina o Keokola ka Smiltsena.
Pilikua o Keokola ka Keoni Komnenos Angelos Doukas Synadenos (Ἰωάννης Κομνηνός Ἄγγελος Δούκας Συναδηνός). O lākou kamaliʻi:





Pīnanaka

Ka pīnanaka ka ʻanoʻano (mai ʻŌlelo ʻInikonekia: "pinang"; ‘Ōlelo Pelekane: areca nut).





ʻIpilapikana

He kumulāʻau ‘o ʻipilapikana (mai ʻŌlelo Tupi: ibirapitanga ; ‘Ōlelo Pelekane: Brazilwood).

Piʻikea

Piʻikea ka aliʻi o Maui a me Hawaiʻi. Ka kaikamahine o Piʻilani (aliʻi nui o Maui) a me La’ieloheloheikawai a me kaikuahine o Lono-a-Piʻilani a me Kiha-a-Piʻilani.
Kāne o Piʻikea ka aliʻi o Hawaiʻi, ʻUmi-a-Līloa. 
O lākou kamaliʻi:





Aʻahaʻapupū

ʻO ke aʻahaʻapupū, ʻo ia ka paʻa ʻana ʻo loko o ka ʻili o ke aʻa koko puʻuwai a hoʻēmi ʻia ke kahe o ke koko.





Arara

ʻO Arara ke kūlanakauhale nui loa o ka hema o Palakila. 13.258 a Arara kanaka.





Radio Studio 54 Network

'O Radio Studio 54 Network he Italia ponoi Radio Station ma muli ma Locri , Calabria . Ka Studio 54 Network ka mea, he FM Radio hana, a ua hōʻike i ka umi'āina i loko o elima wahi o ka hema Ikalia: Catania, Messina, Reggio Calabria, Vibo Valentia, Catanzaro, Cosenza, Crotone, Lecce, Potenza a me Salerno).
Presenters.
Rossella Laface, Alex Albano, Enzo DiChiera, Paolo Sia, Demetrio Malgeri, Marika Torcivia, Franco Siciliano, Mara Rechichi, Luigi Di Dieco





Nanuka

He māmela maiʻao ka nanuka (mai ʻŌlelo Inuinnaqtun: nanuq, inoa Lākina: "Ursus maritimus") o ka ʻohana kālaimeaola ʻo Pōpoki.

Kamailehope

Kolu hōkū 'o Kamailehope aiʻole Alpha Centauri ma ulu hōkū kō Centaurus. Ka hōkū kokoke loa mai ka Lā.





Lehua Kona

He pilikua ʻulaʻula hōkū 'o Lehua Kona aiʻole Alpha Scorpii ma ulu hōkū kō ka Makau Nui o Maui. He kōkoʻo kona kapa ʻia Antares B.





Hōkūpa'a

He hōkū 'o Hōkūpa'a ai'ole Polaris ma ulu hōkū kō Ursa Minor a me Wēlau ʻĀkau kō he lani. He kekahi kōkoʻo kona.





Ka huihui o Makali'i

'O ka huihui o Makali'i ai'ole Messier 45 ma ulu hōkū o Taurus. He kolu kaukani hōkū. He inoa 'alohi (7) hōkū: Alcycone, Atlas, Electra, Maia, Merope, Taygeta a me Pleione.





‘Ilioki

‘O ‘Ilioki he hōkū hele peke nui ma ke kahua o nā hōkū. Lima mahina kona. ‘O Clyde Tombaugh ua loaʻa kēlā.
‘O ʻAkiu lewa lipo New Horizons ua kipa ke hōkū hele peke ʻoiai i makahiki 2015.





Hōkūnohoaupuni

'O Hōkūnohoaupuni he wiliau hōkū. Ka Kahua o nā hōkū a me ma kahi ʻelua hanele piliona hōkū kō loko. 'O waena kōna ma ka ulu hōkū kō ka Pinao.





Māhele:Nā wiliau hōkū






Wiliau hōkū o ʻAnakolomeka

ʻO ʻAnakolomeka he wiliau hōkū ma wele hōkū o ʻAnakolomeka. Ka nui wiliau hōkū ma ka ʻoneʻi huihui wiliau hōkū. Kohu like Hōkūnohoaupuni he kekahi kona.
E hālāwai hoʻokuʻi ana me Hōkūnohoaupuni kēia 3.75 piliona makahiki aʻe.





Mahina

He mea ʻano lani ʻo Mahina. Hoʻomau 'o lā kona a me ala pōʻai Honuapui 29 lā.

’'O Wikipikia ʻĀkia Mahina is about writing Asia. If you are writing five or more pages about Asia, Special design letter(from other country) will send to you. Why don't you join us? If you are interested, please sign this page. If you want to be local organizer, please sign below.
